  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 Transformer 实体追踪模型依赖密集的注意力算子，计算开销巨大。研究人员旨在利用注意力机制中“局部块对角线集中”的结构特性，优化计算效率，以解决长序列建模中的高昂成本问题。

Method: 提出了一种基于块状评估（blockwise evaluation）的注意力算子。通过观察到注意力权重高度集中在块对角线区域，该方法将内部块交互保持精确计算，而将跨块交互映射到一个简化系统中进行处理，从而将复杂度降低至次二次方水平 O(n^{4/3}d)。

Result: 在受控实体追踪基准测试中，该方法在保持与密集算子相同精度的前提下，墙上时间减少了 12-29%。与紧凑型密集 Transformer 相比，在相似精度下速度提升最高达 2.4 倍。同时，研究指出当同时演化的属性数量超过注意力头数时，性能会显著下降。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了利用注意力机制的结构化稀疏性，通过块状评估方法能够有效降低实体追踪任务中的计算复杂度，同时保持高精度。这为在大规模序列处理中实现高效注意力计算提供了重要思路。

Abstract: Entity tracking requires maintaining and updating latent states for entities and attributes over long sequences. Recent task-specific attention operators can compress deep Transformer stacks into a few layers by performing multi-hop state propagation within a single layer, but their dense evaluation remains expensive. We show that in this setting, learned attention is strongly structured: most mass concentrates in local block-diagonal neighborhoods with a light cross-block residue. Exploiting this, we derive a blockwise evaluation of a resolvent-style operator that keeps within-block interactions exact and routes cross-block interactions through a reduced system. The resulting evaluation is subquadratic in sequence length $O(n^{4/3}d)$ (and $O(n^{7/3})$ when $d\approx n$). On controlled tracking benchmarks, our method matches the dense operator's accuracy while reducing wall-clock time by $12-29\%$ under a standardized measurement protocol, and is up to $2.4 \times$ faster than a compact dense Transformer at comparable exact-match accuracy. We further provide ablations over block size and model capacity, and identify a limitation: performance collapses when the number of simultaneously evolving properties exceeds the number of attention heads.

</details>


### [119] [Bandit Convex Optimization with Gradient Prediction Adaptivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22191)
*Shuche Wang,Adarsh Barik,Vincent Y. F. Tan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了带预测信息的Bandit凸优化问题。研究发现单点反馈下无法利用预测优化最差情况，但在双点反馈下，作者提出了TP-VR-OPT算法，通过新型方差缩减估计器，实现了随预测误差自适应的近似最优悔界，并将其推广至非平稳场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的在线凸优化（BCO）仅提供部分反馈，该文旨在研究在存在预测信息（gradient predictions）的情况下，算法是否能实现预测自适应，即悔界是否能随预测误差累积值（S_T）而非仅随时间步长T进行缩放，从而提高最差情况下的性能。

Method: 1. 证明了单点反馈协议下，即使预测误差趋于零，悔界依然存在不可避免的Ω(√T)下界。
2. 在双点反馈设置下，提出了一种新型的“方差缩减乐观梯度下降”（TP-VR-OPT）算法，其核心是一个方差随预测误差缩放而非梯度范数缩放的新型梯度估计器。
3. 建立了信息论下界Ω(√E[S_T])，验证了算法的近似最优性。
4. 进一步开发了无需预知误差或时间长度的自适应变体，并将其扩展至非平稳环境。

Result: 1. 证明了在单点反馈下，预测信息无法克服Ω(√T)的悔界下界。
2. 提出了TP-VR-OPT算法，在双点反馈下实现了O(√(d·E[S_T]))的悔界。
3. 证明了该悔界在信息论意义下达到了近似最优（差因子为√d）。
4. 在非平稳环境下实现了同时适应预测误差和路径长度的动态悔界。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论分析和算法设计，揭示了在双点反馈设置下，利用梯度预测信息实现预测自适应悔界（regret bound）的必要条件与最优性能上限。TP-VR-OPT算法在理论上实现了与信息论下界高度接近的性能，证明了通过方差缩减技术可以有效地将预测误差转化为算法的性能增益。

Abstract: Bandit convex optimization (BCO) is a fundamental online learning framework with partial feedback, where the learner observes only the loss incurred at the chosen decision point in each round. In this work, we investigate whether optimistic gradient predictions can improve worst-case regret guarantees in a prediction-adaptive manner. Specifically, given gradient predictions $m_t$, we seek regret bounds that scale with the cumulative prediction error $S_T=\sum_{t=1}^T \|\nabla f_t(x_t)-m_t\|^2.$ We first establish a negative result: under the single-point feedback protocol, an unavoidable $Ω(\sqrt{T})$ regret lower bound persists even when $S_T=o(T)$, showing that the variance of gradient estimation fundamentally obscures the benefit of accurate predictions. To overcome this barrier, we propose \emph{Two-Point Variance-Reduced Optimistic Gradient Descent} (TP-VR-OPT) for the two-point feedback setting. The key idea is a novel variance-reduced gradient estimator whose variance scales with the prediction error rather than the gradient norm. This yields a regret bound of $O\big(\sqrt{d\,\mathbb{E}[S_T]}\big),$ where $d$ is the decision dimension. Complementing this result, we establish an information-theoretic lower bound that scales as $Ω(\sqrt{\mathbb{E}[S_T]})$, providing a fundamental characterization of the best achievable prediction-adaptive regret and showing that TP-VR-OPT is optimal up to a factor of $\sqrt d$. We further develop adaptive variants that eliminate the need for prior knowledge of $\mathbb{E}[S_T]$ or the horizon $T$, and extend our framework to non-stationary environments, establishing dynamic regret guarantees that adapt simultaneously to the cumulative prediction error and the comparator path length.

</details>

*Manuel Noah Riesen,Peter Alfred von Niederhäusern*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为“强化思维图”（RGoT）的自动化方法。该方法将强化学习（RL）引入思维图（GoT）框架，使模型能够根据任务的复杂性，从预定义的操作集合中自动、自适应地构建出最优的思维操作图。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过强化学习自动构建“思维图”不仅是可行的，而且能够显著增强大语言模型在复杂问题解决中的适应性和灵活性，克服了传统手动定义图结构的局限性。

Abstract: Graph of Thoughts (GoT), a generalized form of recent prompting paradigms for large language models (LLMs), has been shown to be useful for elaborate problem solving. By executing a graph of operations, thoughts of the LLM are structured as an arbitrary graph, forming the actual graph of thoughts. Originally, the graph of operations is defined manually, which requires in-depth knowledge about the solution of the problem to solve. Such a static graph of operations is rigid and therefore lacks adaptability. We propose Reinforced Graph of Thoughts (RGoT), an automated approach to the GoT prompting paradigm that leverages reinforcement learning (RL) to adaptively generate a graph of operations from a human-defined set. Results indicate that, under certain constraints, it is possible to construct graphs of operations adaptively to the task's complexity in an automated way.

### [121] [A Tutorial on Diffusion Theory: From Differential Equations to Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22586)
*Jiayi Fu,Yuxia Wang*

TL;DR: 本文通过微分方程视角对扩散模型进行了深入教程式分析，统一了前向与反向动力学过程，证明了噪声预测与分数匹配的等价性，并厘清了DDPM、DDIM等模型在逆向SDE/ODE框架下的本质联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在通过微分方程的统一视角，深入阐释扩散模型的工作原理，并从理论上统一现有的各种扩散模型框架及采样方法。

Method: 该教程通过分析条件高斯前向过程，推导其对应的常微分方程（ODE）和随机微分方程（SDE）表示，引入边缘分数函数（marginal score）来推导反向动力学，并建立了分数匹配目标函数与噪声预测目标函数的等价性。

Result: 证明了标准噪声预测目标等价于分数匹配；阐明了DDPM与DDIM分别对应于离散的逆向SDE采样和逆向ODE采样，并讨论了包括DPM-Solver在内的多种采样及引导策略。

Abstract: This tutorial develops diffusion models from the viewpoint of differential equations. We begin with the conditional Gaussian forward process and show that this path admits both an ordinary differential equation (ODE) representation and a stochastic differential equation (SDE) representation. Averaging the conditional process over the data distribution then yields marginalized forward ODE and SDE formulations that transport the data distribution $p_0=p_{\mathrm{data}}$ to a Gaussian prior $p_1=\mathcal{N}(0,I)$. We next derive the corresponding reverse-time dynamics, namely the reverse SDE and the reverse probability-flow ODE, both of which are governed by the marginal score $\grad\log p_t(x)$. This leads to a training objective for score estimation and shows that the standard noise-prediction objective is equivalent to score matching up to an additive constant independent of the model parameters. We then discuss sampling methods for the learned reverse dynamics, including DPM-Solver, as well as guided sampling through classifier guidance and classifier-free guidance. Finally, we compare DDPM and DDIM with the reverse SDE/ODE framework and show that they share the same training objective, while DDPM sampling corresponds to discrete reverse-SDE sampling and DDIM sampling corresponds to reverse-ODE sampling.

### [122] [Two is better than one: A Collapse-free Multi-Reward RLIF Training Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22620)
*Shourov Joarder,Diganta Sikdar,Ahsan Habib Akash,Binod Bhattarai,Prashnna Gyawali*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习方法（如RLVR）高度依赖外部监督（人工标注或标准答案），而现有的单奖励RLIF方法存在奖励劫持、熵坍缩及推理结构退化等问题，难以实现高效的无监督学习。

Method: 提出了一种多奖励内部反馈强化学习（RLIF）框架，包含两个核心组件：1. 基于聚类投票的答案级奖励与基于Token级自确定性的完成级奖励；2. 采用基于GDPO的归一化方法来处理奖励规模失衡问题；3. 引入KL-Cov正则化机制，通过缓解低熵分布导致的熵坍缩，从而保障模型在训练后期的探索能力。

Result: 该方法在数学推理和代码生成任务中，表现出比现有无监督RL方法更高的稳定性和鲁棒性，性能水平接近有监督的RLVR方法，有效缓解了模型训练过程中的不稳定性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过结合互补的内部奖励信号与针对性的正则化策略，可以在无需外部监督的情况下，实现稳定且高质量的推理模型训练。该框架为大规模语言模型的无监督推理优化提供了一种高效且鲁棒的范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has substantially improved the reasoning ability of LLMs, but often depends on external supervision from human annotations or gold-standard solutions. Reinforcement learning from internal feedback (RLIF) has recently emerged as a scalable unsupervised alternative, using signals extracted from the model itself. However, existing RLIF methods typically rely on a single internal reward, which can lead to reward hacking, entropy collapse, and degraded reasoning structure. We propose a multi-reward RLIF framework that decomposes the training signal into two complementary components: an answer-level reward based on cluster voting and a completion-level reward based on token-wise self-certainty. To combine these signals robustly, we apply GDPO-based normalization to reduce reward-scale imbalance. We further introduce KL-Cov regularization, which targets low-entropy token distributions responsible for disproportionate entropy reduction, preserving exploration and preventing late-stage collapse. Across mathematical reasoning and code-generation benchmarks, our method improves stability and robustness over prior unsupervised RL approaches, while achieving performance close to supervised RLVR methods. These results show that complementary internal rewards, combined with targeted regularization, can support stable long-horizon reasoning without relying on external ground-truth supervision. Code will be released soon.

### [123] [Can Transformers Learn to Verify During Backtracking Search?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22221)
*Yin Jun Phua,Tony Ribeiro,Tuan Nguyen,Katsumi Inoue*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对Transformer在搜索任务中过度依赖历史轨迹的问题，提出了“选择性状态注意力（SSA）”，通过结构化约束强制模型仅根据当前搜索状态进行决策，有效消除了历史信息的干扰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前Transformer模型通过拟合离线求解器轨迹进行训练，以学习回溯搜索策略。然而，研究发现模型并未充分利用搜索状态的马尔可夫性质，而是过度依赖历史轨迹，导致其在面对相同状态但不同路径时无法做出一致的预测。为了解决这一逻辑缺陷，作者旨在构建能够纯粹基于当前搜索状态进行决策的模型架构。

Method: 1. 诊断：分析了Transformer在处理串行搜索轨迹数据时存在的“分散检索”（scattered retrieval）和“历史纠缠”（history entanglement）问题。
2. 修复方案：
   - 局部化（Localization）：重写决策块，将关键状态特征局部化。
   - 选择性状态注意力（Selective State Attention, SSA）：通过固定的注意力掩码强制模型仅基于当前状态进行决策，无需更改训练目标或模型参数。

Result: 在3-SAT、图着色、积木世界和回溯解析等任务中，实验结果显示：相比于传统的累积训练基线，使用SSA的模型在面对相同状态但不同历史的决策输入时，能够输出高度一致的预测，证明了SSA成功解耦了历史轨迹干扰，并实现了基于状态的决策优化。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了基于累积轨迹训练的Transformer在处理搜索决策时存在状态表示分散和历史依赖纠缠的问题。通过引入局部化（Localization）和选择性状态注意力（SSA）机制，能够在保持结构化决策的同时，消除无关历史对模型预测的干扰，为提升大模型在搜索与推理任务中的鲁棒性提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Backtracking search underlies classical constraint solvers, planners, and theorem provers. Recent transformer-based reasoning systems explore search trees over their own intermediate steps. A common training recipe fits an autoregressive next-token loss on offline solver traces. The model's input at each step is a cumulative trace of all prior decisions. The optimal continue-or-backtrack predictor depends only on the current search state, since two trajectories reaching the same state admit the same viable continuations. We show that decoder-only transformers trained on cumulative traces fail this requirement in two ways: the trace can scatter state features across many positions (scattered retrieval), and the predictor can condition on the trajectory rather than the state (history entanglement). We address scattered retrieval with localization, a trace-level fix that rewrites each decision block to expose state features locally. We address history entanglement with Selective State Attention (SSA), a fixed attention mask that enforces state-based decisions structurally without modifying training data, objective, or parameters. We focus on reactive verification, after propagation has exposed a contradiction. We test SSA on 3-SAT, graph coloring, Blocks World, and backtracking parsing. On same-state pairs that differ only in prior history, SSA emits identical decisions while a cumulative-trained causal baseline does not. Our contribution is a diagnostic of transformer behavior on serialized trajectory data, paired with a structural fix. Pretrained language models that search over their own reasoning steps may face the same failure. Our analysis opens up inference-time context clearing as a candidate way to apply the same isolation without retraining.

</details>


### [124] [How Many Different Outputs Can a Transformer Generate?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22223)
*Maxime Meyer,Mario Michelessa,Caroline Chaux,Vincent Y. F. Tan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 定量分析：结合Transformer架构参数（如提示词长度），构建序列输出数量的数学上限模型。
2. 实验验证：通过跨不同架构和模型规模的实验，验证所提出的上限模型的紧密程度。

2. 发现序列长度超过某一临界阈值后，可访问序列的比例呈指数级衰减。
3. 提出了一个理论上限，证明该上限在多种模型架构和规模下具有极高的紧密性（误差在10倍以内）。
4. 上述结论在无限上下文和无限计算时间的条件下依然成立。

Conclusion: 该研究从理论上阐明了Transformer输出能力的局限性。研究表明，Transformer能够生成的序列数量受到提示词长度的严格制约，即使在无限上下文和计算时间的理想条件下，其输出空间也呈指数级衰减。这解释了Transformer在处理复制或记忆等简单序列任务时表现出的性能瓶颈，为理解模型生成能力的边界提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: We study how we can leverage only a handful of characteristics of a transformer's architecture to closely predict the number of different sequences it can output, both qualitatively and quantitatively. We provide an upper bound depending on the length of the prompt, which we show empirically to be tight up to a factor less than 10, across architectures and model sizes. Our analysis also provides a theoretical explanation for previously observed empirical failures of transformers on simple sequence tasks, such as copying and cramming. Formally, we prove that (i) the maximal length of accessible sequences (those that the transformer can output for some prompt) grows linearly with the prompt length, (ii) beyond a critical threshold, the proportion of accessible sequences decays exponentially with sequence length, and (iii) the linear coefficient relating prompt length to accessible sequence length admits a theoretical upper bound. Notably, these results hold even with unbounded context and computation time.

### [125] [Vector Policy Optimization: Training for Diversity Improves Test-Time Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22817)
*Ryan Bahlous-Boldi,Isha Puri,Idan Shenfeld,Akarsh Kumar,Mehul Damani,Sebastian Risi,Omar Khattab,Zhang-Wei Hong,Pulkit Agrawal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型后训练中因标量奖励优化导致的“多样性不足”问题，本文提出了向量策略优化（VPO），通过在向量化奖励空间中训练模型生成多样化的解决方案，显著提升了模型在推理时搜索（如AlphaEvolve）中的性能与适应能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM后训练范式主要针对标量奖励进行优化，这导致模型生成的响应分布熵较低，缺乏多样性。然而，随着模型越来越多地被应用于需要推理时搜索（Inference-time search）的场景，这种低多样性限制了模型在复杂任务中通过搜索寻找更优解的能力。因此，需要一种能够显式训练模型产生多样化解空间的策略。

Method: 提出向量策略优化（Vector Policy Optimization, VPO）。VPO是GRPO优势估计器的直接替代方案，其核心在于将单标量奖励优化扩展为向量化奖励空间优化。通过训练模型生成针对不同向量化奖励维度（如代码生成的不同测试用例、不同用户偏好）特化的解决方案，从而在保持多样性的同时提升搜索效率。

Result: 在四个任务中，VPO在测试时搜索指标（如pass@k和best@k）上均达到或优于现有的最强标量强化学习基线，且随着搜索预算的增加，性能差距进一步扩大。在演化搜索任务中，VPO模型能够解决GRPO模型无法处理的复杂问题。

Conclusion: 多样性对于推理时搜索至关重要。VPO提供了一种针对推理阶段需求进行预训练的方法，通过优化向量化奖励空间，使得模型能够生成更多样化的解决方案，从而在测试时搜索（如AlphaEvolve等）中展现出更强的适应性和性能。多样性优化可能成为未来大语言模型后训练的核心范式。

Abstract: Language models must now generalize out of the box to novel environments and work inside inference-scaling search procedures, such as AlphaEvolve, that select rollouts with a variety of task-specific reward functions. Unfortunately, the standard paradigm of LLM post-training optimizes a pre-specified scalar reward, often leading current LLMs to produce low-entropy response distributions and thus to struggle at displaying the diversity that inference-time search will require. We propose Vector Policy Optimization (VPO), an RL algorithm that explicitly trains policies to anticipate diverse downstream reward functions and to produce diverse solutions. VPO exploits that rewards are often vector-valued in practice, like per-test-case correctness in code generation or, say, multiple different user personas or reward models. VPO is essentially a drop-in replacement for the GRPO advantage estimator, but it trains the LLM to output a set of solutions where individual solutions specialize to different trade-offs in the vector reward space. Across four tasks, VPO matches or beats the strongest scalar RL baselines on test-time search (e.g. pass@k and best@k), with the gap widening as the search budget grows. For evolutionary search, VPO models unlock problems that GRPO models cannot solve at all. As test-time search becomes more standardized, optimizing for diversity may need to become the default post-training objective.

</details>


### [126] [Decomposing Ensemble Spread in Lorenz '96 With Learned Stochastic Parameterizations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22242)
*Birgit Kühbacher,Daan Crommelin,Niki Kilbertus*

Result: 研究发现集合扰动并不增加系统的长期方差，而是调节了轨迹去相关及遍历不变测度的速度。其中，具有时间持续结构的随机参数化方案能显著增强早期的离散度增长，并有效改善预报离散度与误差之间的一致性。

Abstract: Weather and climate forecasts are inherently uncertain due to chaotic dynamics, imperfect initial conditions, and incomplete representation of the underlying physical processes. Operational ensemble forecasts aim to represent these uncertainties through forecast spread, yet many approaches yield underdispersive estimates, with spread that grows too slowly relative to forecast error. Using the two-scale Lorenz 1996 system as a widely used, controlled testbed, we design a systematic approach to disentangle intrinsic variability, initial-condition perturbations, and stochastic model uncertainty. We compare multiple ensemble configurations and parameterization strategies, including existing deterministic and autoregressive as well as novel Bayesian and flow-based approaches. Our results show that ensemble perturbations do not increase the system's long-term variance; rather, they regulate how rapidly trajectories decorrelate and explore the invariant measure. Stochastic parameterizations, particularly those with temporally persistent structure, enhance early spread growth and improve spread-error consistency. Overall, we bring clarity to how different sources of uncertainty interact in a chaotic system and provide guidance for the design and evaluation of stochastic parameterizations in weather and climate models.

Abstract: Predictive modelling is important for health data analysis and data-driven clinical decision-making. ### [128] [What are the Right Symmetries for Formal Theorem Proving?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22257)
*Krzysztof Olejniczak,Radoslav Dimitrov,Xingyue Huang,Bernardo Cuenca Grau,Jinwoo Kim,İsmail İlkan Ceylan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的LLM形式化定理证明器对问题表述的微小变动极度敏感，缺乏对形式数学中结构对称性的尊重，导致语义等价的命题在证明成功率上表现出巨大差异。

Method: 引入“重写范畴”（rewriting categories）框架，用范畴论形式化定义“证明等变性”和“成功不变性”；分析基于状态的证明器与LLM证明器在这些属性上的差异；提出在推理阶段通过聚合输入的等价重写形式来逼近成功不变性的方法。

Result: 研究发现LLM证明器未能满足证明等变性和成功不变性，导致性能波动；实验表明，通过在推理时聚合等价重写形式，可以在固定预算下显著提升证明器的鲁棒性和成功率。

Conclusion: 本文通过范畴论框架揭示了形式化定理证明中对称性的重要性，强调了对称性是LLM证明器缺失的关键归纳偏置。通过推理阶段的重写聚合方法，可以有效近似这种对称性，从而提升证明器的鲁棒性和性能。

Abstract: Formal theorem provers based on large language models (LLMs) are highly sensitive to superficial variations in problem representation: semantically equivalent statements can exhibit drastically different proof success rates, revealing a failure to respect structural symmetries inherent in formal mathematics. This raises a central question: what are the right symmetries for formal theorem proving? We introduce rewriting categories, a category-theoretic framework capturing the compositional, generally non-invertible transformations induced by proof tactics, and use it to formalize two symmetry notions: proof equivariance, governing how proof distributions transform under rewrites, and success invariance (i.e., invariance of success probability), requiring equivalent statements to be solved with the same probability. We observe that state-based next-tactic provers naturally satisfy proof equivariance by operating on proof states. In contrast, state-of-the-art LLM-based provers satisfy neither property, exhibiting large performance variation across equivalent formulations. To mitigate this, we propose test-time methods that aggregate over equivalent rewritings of the input, showing theoretically that they recover success invariance in the sampling limit, and empirically, that they improve robustness and performance under fixed inference budgets. Our results highlight symmetry as a key missing inductive bias in LLM-based theorem proving and suggest test-time computation as a practical route to approximate it.

### [130] [Tailoring Teaching to Aptitude: Direction-Adaptive Self-Distillation for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22263)
*Hongbin Zhang,Chaozheng Wang,Kehai Chen,Youcheng Pan,Yang Xiang,Jinpeng Wang,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对大模型自蒸馏中因监督单一化导致的推理能力下降问题，提出了DASD（方向自适应自蒸馏）方法。该方法根据Token的熵值动态调整监督方向，平衡了模型的探索能力与执行准确性，显著提升了数学推理任务的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有同质化在线自蒸馏（OPSD）范式强制模型在所有Token上遵循统一监督，这抑制了模型在复杂推理任务中所需的预测不确定性和假设修正能力，导致模型性能退化。需要一种能根据不确定性水平动态调整监督策略的方法。

Method: 提出方向自适应自蒸馏（DASD）方法。其核心思想是将基于特权信息的均匀教师监督转化为“熵路由”的方向性监督：针对高熵（高不确定性）Token，鼓励模型偏离教师以维持探索空间；针对低熵（低不确定性）Token，强制模型趋向教师以确保执行准确性。

Result: 在六个数学推理基准测试中，DASD在宏观Avg@16指标上均优于现有的强基准模型（如RLVR和传统自蒸馏方法）。通过Pass@k和推理健康度分析证明，DASD在保持探索性的同时，未牺牲步骤级执行的准确性。

Conclusion: DASD证明了通过熵引导的差异化监督策略，可以在大模型自蒸馏过程中平衡探索与精确执行。该方法有效解决了传统同质化自蒸馏导致模型复杂推理能力退化的问题，为大模型推理能力的后训练优化提供了一种更精细、更有效的范式。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) is an emerging LLM post-training paradigm in which the model serves as its own teacher: conditioned on privileged information such as a reference trace or hint, the same policy provides dense token-level supervision on its own rollouts. However, recent studies show that OPSD degrades complex reasoning by suppressing predictive uncertainty, which supports exploration and hypothesis revision. Our token-level analysis shows that this failure arises from applying a uniform direction of teacher supervision across tokens with different uncertainty levels: conformity to the privileged self-teacher suppresses exploration at high entropy, while deviation from the teacher degrades step accuracy at low entropy. Accordingly, we propose \textbf{Direction-Adaptive Self-Distillation} (\textbf{DASD}), which reframes privileged self-distillation from uniform teacher imitation into entropy-routed directional supervision: high-entropy tokens are pushed away from the privileged teacher to preserve exploration, while low-entropy tokens are pulled toward the teacher to stabilize step-level execution. Across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks, DASD achieves the best macro Avg@16 over strong RLVR and self-distillation baselines. Pass@$k$, reasoning-health, and generalization analyses show that these average gains come from preserving exploration without sacrificing step-level execution.

### [131] [Detecting Atypical Clients in Federated Learning via Representation-Level Divergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22266)
*Cristian Pérez-Corral,Jose I. Mestre,Alberto Fernández-Hernández,Manuel F. Dolz,Enrique S. Quitana-Ortí*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于输入空间激活划分的轻量级几何指标，通过量化客户端与全局模型的功能偏差，有效识别联邦学习中的异常更新，提升了系统的可靠性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在联邦学习中，客户端数据的非独立同分布（non-i.i.d.）导致数据异构，引发更新不稳定和性能下降。此外，实际部署中存在分布偏移和异常输入问题，导致客户端更新偏离预期，亟需一种可靠的方法来监控客户端行为并提升聚合过程的鲁棒性。

Method: 研究人员提出了一种轻量级的几何信号方法，不再直接比较模型参数或梯度，而是通过共享探针集（probe set），衡量各客户端在本地训练后如何改变模型输入空间的“激活诱导划分”（activation-induced partition）。该度量具有置换不变性（permutation-invariant），能够捕捉模型处理数据方式的差异。

Result: 实验表明，该几何信号能够有效识别导致非典型功能变化的客户端，并成功区分异构但在稳定范围内的客户端与那些显著背离全局模式的异常客户端。基于此度量，可以实现更具风险意识（risk-aware）的聚合策略。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于激活空间划分的几何信号能够有效量化客户端与全局模型之间的功能偏差，为联邦学习系统提供了一种简单、可解释且鲁棒的监控与聚合策略工具，有效缓解了数据异构性和异常更新带来的负面影响。

Abstract: Federated learning enables collaborative training across distributed clients with heterogeneous data, but such heterogeneity often leads to unstable updates and degraded global performance. Moreover, in practical deployments, client updates may deviate from the expected behavior not only due to benign not i.i.d. distributions, but also due to distributional shifts or anomalous inputs, raising concerns about the reliability of the aggregation process. In this work, we propose a lightweight geometric signal to quantify the functional deviation of a client with respect to the global model. Instead of comparing model parameters or gradients, our approach measures how the local training of each client alters the activation-induced partition of the input space, evaluated on a shared probe set. This yields a permutation-invariant, interpretable metric of client--global divergence that captures differences in how data is processed by the model. We show that this signal effectively identifies clients that induce atypical functional changes, distinguishing stable yet heterogeneous clients from those whose updates significantly diverge from the global regime. As a result, the proposed metric provides a simple tool for monitoring client behavior and enabling risk-aware aggregation strategies in federated learning systems.

</details>


### [132] [Adaptive Measurement Allocation for Learning Kernelized SVMs Under Noisy Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22275)
*Artur Miroszewski*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对噪声环境下的核方法，提出了一种基于几何敏感性和主动集不稳定性的自适应测量分配策略，通过将测量预算集中于决策关键区域，显著提高了在量子计算等含噪观测场景下的分类性能和预算使用效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有核方法通常假设核矩阵是无噪的。然而，在量子机器学习等新兴领域，核矩阵条目是通过含噪观测估算的。传统的均匀测量分配方法忽略了核化分类器对核矩阵各条目的非均匀依赖性，导致测量预算利用率低下。因此，需要一种能够感知决策关键区域的自适应测量策略。

Method: 1. 提出了一种针对含噪伯努利观测的学习核支持向量机（SVM）的自适应测量分配策略。
2. 引入了两个核心原则：(i) 几何敏感性，用于捕捉核矩阵扰动对分类器边际的影响；(ii) 主动集不稳定性，用于量化噪声导致的支撑向量成员资格变化的概率。
3. 利用上述信号定义了一种任务感知的分配方案，并开发了基于对偶系数稳定性的提前停止准则。

Result: 1. 理论分析表明，自适应分配的收益取决于核重要性结构的异质性，并定义了自适应策略优于均匀策略的适用场景。
2. 实验证明，在固定预算下，该方法显著提升了支撑向量恢复、边际估计及决策函数的精度。
3. 提前停止准则能够以极少的测量成本获得接近最优的性能。
4. 在量子核实验中，该方法表现出与核集中现象一致的区域依赖行为。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了自适应测量分配策略优于传统的均匀分配策略。通过结合几何敏感性和主动集不稳定性，该方法能够将有限的测量预算集中于对决策边界影响最大的核矩阵区域，从而在量子机器学习等存在观测噪声的场景下，以更低的成本实现更高的分类性能。

Abstract: Kernel methods are typically formulated under the assumption of exact, noise-free access to the Gram matrix. However, in emerging settings such as quantum machine learning, each kernel entry must be inferred from noisy observations, and its accuracy depends on how a limited measurement budget is allocated. Despite this, existing approaches overwhelmingly rely on uniform allocation, which equalizes estimator variance but ignores the highly non-uniform dependence of kernelized classifiers on the Gram matrix. In this work, we introduce an adaptive measurement-allocation strategy for learning kernelized Support Vector Machines (SVMs) from noisy Bernoulli observations. Our approach combines two complementary principles: (i) geometric sensitivity, capturing how perturbations of individual kernel entries affect the classifier margin, and (ii) active-set instability, quantifying the probability of discrete changes in support-vector membership induced by measurement noise. These signals define a task-aware allocation scheme that concentrates measurements on the most decision-critical regions of the kernel matrix. We provide a theoretical analysis showing that the benefit of adaptive allocation is governed by the heterogeneity of the induced kernel importance structure, leading to distinct regimes in which adaptive or uniform strategies are preferable. Empirical evaluations on synthetic datasets demonstrate that adaptive allocation significantly improves support-vector recovery, margin estimation, and decision-function accuracy under fixed measurement budgets. A dual-coefficient stability criterion further enables early stopping, achieving near-optimal performance while using only a fraction of the measurement cost. ### [134] [One LR Doesn't Fit All: Heavy-Tail Guided Layerwise Learning Rates for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22297)
*Di He,Songjun Tu,Keyu Wang,Lu Yin,Shiwei Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对Transformer架构中各层训练不平衡的问题，本文提出了一种基于重尾自正则化理论的层级学习率（LLR）方法，通过自适应分配各层学习率，显著提升了训练速度与大语言模型的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代深度学习中普遍采用的“统一学习率”策略忽视了Transformer模型不同层之间的结构异质性，限制了大语言模型（LLM）的训练效率与性能表现。作者旨在通过自适应调整各层学习率，克服这种局限性，实现更均衡的训练过程。

Method: 本文提出了“层级学习率（LLR）”方法，该方法基于重尾自正则化（HT-SR）理论，利用权重相关矩阵的经验谱密度（ESD）来量化各层的重尾特性。具体策略为：对重尾特性较弱的层分配较大的学习率以加速收敛，对重尾特性较强的层分配较小的学习率以确保稳定性，从而实现各层的平衡训练。

Result: 实验表明，LLR在多种架构（LLaMA至GPT-nano）、优化器（AdamW与Muon）及参数规模（60M-1B）下均表现优异。相比基线模型，LLR实现了最高1.5倍的训练加速，并将平均零样本准确率从47.09%提升至49.02%，且具有较低的调参开销。

Conclusion: 本文提出的层级学习率（LLR）策略通过理论驱动的自适应调整，有效地解决了Transformer模型中各层训练不平衡的问题，证明了根据权重矩阵的谱特性调整学习率是提升大模型训练效率与性能的有效途径，且具备良好的通用性与迁移性。

Abstract: Learning rate configuration is a fundamental aspect of modern deep learning. The prevailing practice of applying a uniform learning rate across all layers overlooks the structural heterogeneity of Transformers, potentially limiting their effectiveness as the backbone of Large Language Models (LLMs). In this paper, we introduce Layerwise Learning Rate (LLR), an adaptive scheme that assigns distinct learning rates to individual Transformer layers. Our method is grounded in Heavy-Tailed Self-Regularization (HT-SR) theory, which characterizes the empirical spectral density (ESD) of weight correlation matrices to quantify heavy-tailedness. Layers with weaker heavy-tailedness are assigned larger learning rates to accelerate their training, while layers with stronger heavy-tailedness receive smaller learning rates. By tailoring learning rates in this manner, LLR promotes balanced training across layers, leading to faster convergence and improved generalization. Extensive experiments across architectures (from LLaMA to GPT-nano), optimizers (AdamW and Muon), and parameter scales (60M-1B) demonstrate that LLR achieves up to 1.5x training speedup and outperforms baselines, notably raising average zero-shot accuracy from 47.09% to 49.02%. A key advantage of LLR is its low tuning overhead: it transfers nearly optimal LR settings directly from the uniform baseline. Code is available at https://github.com/hed-ucas/Layer-wise-Learning-Rate.

</details>

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种可扩展的、模块化的临床AI部署框架，并证实了在临床推理任务中存在性能与资源配置之间的“U型”缩放规律。该平台为解决临床AI从研究原型到实际部署的系统级障碍提供了实用的架构参考。

Abstract: Despite strong predictive results in the clinical machine learning literature, the translation of these models into bedside use remains limited by systems-level barriers: heterogeneous data representations, the absence of standardized deployment workflows, and a mismatch between research prototypes and the concurrency and latency requirements of hospital environments. A previously validated LightGBM model (F1 0.87-0.94 on PhysioNet 2019) is reused without modification; the contribution lies in the surrounding infrastructure and its empirical characterization under load. Using k6 with 50-1000 concurrent virtual users, we find that replica count must be matched to the physical CPU thread count of the host: scaling from 3 to 12 replicas on a 12-thread CPU reduces p95 latency from 3.3s to 1.41s (57.3% reduction) and eliminates all request failures, while over-provisioning to 24 or 48 replicas degrades performance due to scheduler contention.   To bridge these perspectives, we study how to simultaneously infer and enforce causal structure in the form of topological variable orderings into tabular prediction. Unlike standard architectures, our model TabOrder uses causal order-constrained attention, basing predictions only on features that precede a target under a learned causal order. Abstract: Reconstructing continuous physical fields from sparse measurements is a central inverse problem, but data-driven generative models can produce states that violate governing dynamics. We introduce a physics-informed generative solver that separates stable prior learning from inference-time enforcement of conservation laws. Martingale-Regularized Score Matching regularizes score pretraining with a Score Fokker-Planck constraint, yielding a dynamically stable prior. Physics-Informed Implicit Score Sampling then guides denoising trajectories by gradients of physical residuals, projecting samples toward admissible manifolds without retraining. In acoustics, the method co-generates pressure and particle velocity from sparse sensors, enabling dense virtual arrays that suppress spatial aliasing. Together, this work establishes a rigorous and generalizable paradigm for solving high-dimensional inverse problems, bridging the gap between generative artificial intelligence and first-principles science.

In practice, time-resolved scRNA-seq is collected at only a few discrete time points as unpaired snapshot populations, leaving substantial temporal gaps. This motivates trajectory inference at unmeasured time points. Existing methods mainly follow two directions, optimal-transport (OT) alignment provides distribution-level matching between observed snapshots, while continuous-time generative models support forecasting via learned dynamics. However, two challenges remain: (i) unpaired snapshots render local transitions between adjacent time points ambiguous, leading to unstable supervision; and (ii) long-horizon prediction relies on repeated integration, where small modeling errors compound and cause distribution drift. To address these challenges, we propose single-cell Flow Matching (scFM), a latent generative framework based on coupling-conditioned flow matching. First, we compute entropically regularized OT couplings between adjacent snapshots and use them to construct soft, weighted flow-matching targets for learning time-dependent velocity fields. Second, we learn bidirectional velocity fields and leverage their consistency to refine couplings and improve temporal coherence under sparse supervision. Third, we introduce distribution-level alignment and latent dynamic regularization to anchor long rollouts and mitigate drift. Experiments on real-world time-series scRNA-seq datasets show that scFM consistently improves distributional prediction performance for both temporal interpolation and extrapolation. Moreover, scFM yields more accurate trajectory reconstruction and temporally coherent visualizations where intermediate time points are absent, indicating a more faithful recovery of underlying temporal gene expression dynamics.

To address this, we propose VeriScale, a novel framework driven by the adversarial implementations. It consists of two stages: test-suite expansion to construct diverse and challenging test cases, and test-suite reduction to distill them into compact yet discriminative suites. ### [140] [ASAP: Attention Sink Anchored Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22372)
*Jaehyuk Lee,Hanyoung Kim,Yanggee Kim,Donghun Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为ASAP的视觉Transformer令牌剪枝框架，通过将注意力汇聚点视为信息流的核心，利用随机游走和扩散距离进行令牌聚类与压缩，在无需额外训练的前提下，显著降低了计算复杂性并提升了推理速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ViT在高分辨率下自注意力计算的二次复杂度带来了严重的计算瓶颈；现有的令牌缩减方法依赖于单层局部指标，容易受到“注意力汇聚”现象的干扰，导致无关令牌被保留而显著目标被剔除。

Method: 提出了一种无需训练的框架ASAP。其核心思想是将ViT的信息流建模为“惰性随机游走”（Lazy Random Walk），并将“注意力汇聚”识别为概率质量的累积中心。通过计算累积转移矩阵中令牌到汇聚点的扩散距离，利用径向扩散聚类（Radial Diffusion Clustering）进行令牌分区，并结合转移权重池化（Transition Weight Pooling）来压缩背景冗余。

Result: 在图像、视频和视觉-语言任务的广泛实验中，ASAP表现优于现有的前沿方法，在保持甚至提升基线准确率的同时，将吞吐量提升了高达48%。

Conclusion: ASAP证明了将“注意力汇聚”（Attention Sink）视为特征而非缺陷是有效的，通过将ViT的信息流建模为惰性随机游走，实现了无需训练的高效令牌剪枝，为视觉Transformer的推理加速提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Vision Transformers (ViTs) face severe computational bottlenecks due to the quadratic complexity of self-attention at high resolutions. Existing token reduction methods rely on local metrics - such as single-layer attention scores - that are inherently vulnerable to the attention sink phenomenon, where uninformative tokens are paradoxically preserved over salient foreground objects. We propose ASAP (Attention Sink Anchored Pruning), a training-free framework that recasts this sink as a feature. Modeling ViT information flow as a Lazy Random Walk, ASAP identifies the sink as a dominant accumulator of probability mass. By computing the diffusion distance to the sink within the cumulative transition matrix, ASAP partitions tokens via Radial Diffusion Clustering and compresses background redundancy through Transition Weight Pooling in a single shot. Extensive experiments across image, video, and vision-language tasks demonstrate ASAP outperforms state-of-the-art methods, accelerating throughput by up to 48% while maintaining - or even exceeding - baseline accuracy.

</details>


### [141] [Target-Aligned Bellman Backup for Cross-domain Offline Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22376)
*Wei Liu,Ting Long*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有跨域离线强化学习中基于转换相似度迁移的局限性，本文提出 TABB 方法，通过评估源域数据与目标域贝尔曼目标的对齐程度来选择性迁移数据，有效解决了跨域策略学习中的负迁移问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的跨域离线强化学习（CDRL）方法多采用基于转换相似度的策略进行数据迁移，但视觉或动力学上的相似并不代表长远回报的一致性，这种粗糙的过滤方式容易引入噪声，误导策略学习。作者旨在通过更底层的贝尔曼目标一致性来衡量数据的可迁移性。

Method: 提出了“目标对齐贝尔曼备份”（Target-Aligned Bellman Backup, TABB）方法。该方法不再依赖表面的转换相似度，而是通过评估源域转换对目标域贝尔曼目标估计的贡献度，从而进行选择性的数据利用，确保源域数据能对目标域策略优化起到正面作用。

Result: 在多种跨域离线强化学习设置及目标域数据极其受限的场景下，TABB 方法均表现出了一致且强劲的性能，优于现有的基准方法。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了基于贝尔曼目标对齐的策略比传统的基于转换相似度的方法更能有效利用跨域数据，显著提升了目标域数据稀缺情况下的离线强化学习效果。

Abstract: Cross-domain offline reinforcement learning (CDRL) aims to improve policy learning in a target domain by leveraging data collected from a source domain. Existing works typically assess the transferability of source-domain data by measuring its similarity to target-domain transitions, and implicitly perform transition-level selection. Transitions that are considered similar are assigned higher weights or rewards, while dissimilar ones are down-weighted. However, transition-level similarity does not necessarily imply consistency in long-term returns. Even visually or dynamically similar transitions may lead to significantly different outcomes in the target domain, which can mislead policy learning and degrade performance. To address this issue, we revisit the fundamental objective of policy learning. Since policy optimization ultimately relies on Bellman targets to evaluate the quality of decisions, we propose to assess the transferability of source-domain transitions based on their alignment with target-domain Bellman targets, rather than superficial transition similarity. Based on this insight, we propose a method termed Target-Aligned Bellman Backup (TABB), which selectively leverages source-domain data by measuring their contribution to accurate Bellman target estimation in the target domain. We evaluate TABB across a broad range of cross-domain offline RL settings with highly limited target-domain data. Experimental results show that TABB consistently achieves strong performance.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种结合Kolmogorov-Arnold Networks (KAN) 与 XGBoost 的混合预测框架。该模型利用KAN捕捉全局非线性特征，同时利用XGBoost的树模型增强局部稳定性，并采用扩展窗口策略在澳大利亚国家电力市场（NEM）数据上进行验证。

This paper investigates week-ahead electricity price forecasting and proposes a hybrid KAN+XGBoost framework that integrates Kolmogorov-Arnold Networks (KAN) with tree-based learning. The proposed approach combines the global nonlinear representation capability of KAN with the local robustness of XGBoost to capture both long-term dependencies and short-term price fluctuations. Experiments are conducted on real-world NEM data using an expanding window evaluation strategy. The results demonstrate that the proposed model outperforms benchmark methods, including SARIMAX, Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM), standalone KAN, and XGBoost, reducing MAE by approximately 12% compared to XGBoost and by over 50% compared to a naive baseline. The results suggest that hybrid learning strategies provide an effective and robust solution for electricity price forecasting in highly dynamic electricity markets.

### [143] [AMUSE: Anytime Muon with Stable Gradient Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22432)
*Jueun Kim,Baekrok Shin,Jihun Yun,Beomhan Baek,Minhak Song,Chulhee Yun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文分析了 Muon 优化器在高曲率“峡谷”景观中的振荡缺陷，并提出了 AMUSE 算法。它结合了 Muon 的快速收敛特性与 Schedule-Free 的平均化稳定性，实现了无调度的高效训练，并在多项任务中超越了现有先进优化器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代深度学习常用的 AdamW 优化器依赖预设学习率调度。近期的 Schedule-Free 和 Muon 方法虽然提升了性能，但 Muon 缺乏对“峡谷”损失景观机制的深入理解，且容易产生振荡。研究旨在解决如何结合 Muon 的快速收敛与 Schedule-Free 的稳定性，并消除对学习率调度的依赖。

Method: 提出了一种名为 AMUSE (Anytime MUon with Stable gradient Evaluation) 的算法。该方法通过引入随时间变化的插值系数，在训练初期侧重于 Muon 的快速梯度下降，随后逐渐转向由 Schedule-Free 提供的平均化序列，从而既利用了 Muon 在平坦子空间（“河流”）上的快速进展，又通过平均化抑制了高曲率方向（“峡谷壁”）带来的振荡。

Result: 在视觉任务和大型语言模型预训练实验中，AMUSE 在性能-迭代次数的帕累托前沿（Pareto frontier）上均优于 Schedule-Free AdamW 和 Muon，展现出更好的训练效率和稳定性。

Conclusion: AMUSE 有效融合了 Muon 的快速优化能力与 Schedule-Free 的稳定性，证明了通过动态调整优化轨迹，可以在无需预设学习率调度的情况下，实现更高效、更稳定的模型训练。

Abstract: Modern deep learning commonly relies on AdamW with prescribed learning rate schedules, but recent works challenge both components: Schedule-Free optimization removes explicit schedules via iterate averaging, and Muon improves the update geometry by orthogonalizing momentum for matrix parameters. Despite Muon's strong empirical performance, its underlying mechanism remains partially understood. We study Muon through the river-valley loss landscape, where useful training progress occurs along a flat, low-curvature bulk subspace (the river), while high-curvature dominant directions form steep valley walls that induce oscillations. We empirically show that while Muon's orthogonalization accelerates river progress by increasing the bulk component, it also amplifies dominant-direction noise, causing oscillatory trajectories. Building on this, we propose Anytime MUon with Stable gradient Evaluation (AMUSE), which integrates Muon's rapid bulk progress with the stabilizing effect of Schedule-Free averaging. AMUSE uses a time-varying interpolation coefficient that initially evaluates gradients near the fast Muon sequence for rapid adaptation, then gradually shifts toward the stable averaged sequence to suppress valley-wall oscillations. As a result, AMUSE requires no learning rate schedules and supports anytime training. Across vision tasks and large language model pretraining, AMUSE consistently improves the performance-iteration Pareto frontier over (Schedule-Free) AdamW and Muon.

### [144] [Understanding Multimodal Failure in Action-Chunking Behavioral Cloning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22493)
*Lorenzo Mazza,Massimiliano Datres,Ariel Rodriguez,Sebastian Bodenstedt,Gitta Kutyniok,Stefanie Speidel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了多模态行为克隆中的难点，指出潜变量策略和生成式策略在解决动作多模态问题时各有利弊：前者受正则化程度制约，后者受限于映射的平滑性要求，两者均难以完美覆盖多种动作模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在行为克隆中，同一观测状态下往往存在多种有效的动作选择（即多模态问题），这导致传统单一映射的策略难以有效拟合数据。研究旨在探究现有针对动作分块（action-chunking）的多模态参数化方法在处理该问题时的失效机制及局限性。

Method: 作者深入分析了潜变量策略（latent-variable policies）与动作空间生成式策略（action-space generative policies）的数学特性。前者通过探讨后验-先验正则化对采样可靠性的影响来建模；后者通过利普希茨常数约束下的基到动作传输映射来分析多模态生成的局限性，并通过合成任务和机器人仿真实验进行验证。

Result: 实验表明，过度正则化会导致潜变量模型丢失区分不同动作模态的信息，而若正则化不足则导致采样不可靠；对于生成式策略，若要覆盖多个分散的模态，则必须在基空间中引入剧烈的转换或在动作空间中存在非支持的过渡区域，这限制了模型的学习效果。

Conclusion: 该研究阐明了多模态行为克隆中存在的内在权衡：潜变量模型需要在后验-先验正则化强度与保留模态区分信息之间取得平衡；而基于生成式的策略则受限于映射的利普希茨常数（Lipschitz constant），难以在保持平滑性的同时覆盖多个分离的动作模式。

Abstract: Behavioral cloning becomes difficult when the same observation admits several valid actions. We study this problem for action-chunking policies and show that different multimodal parameterizations fail in different ways. For latent-variable policies, posterior-prior regularization makes deployment-time sampling more reliable, but excessive regularization removes the action-conditioned information needed to distinguish demonstrated modes. Reducing this regularization can preserve mode information, but then success depends on whether the prior covers the relevant latent regions. For action-space generative policies, multimodality is constrained by the smoothness of the base-to-action transport: a map with small Lipschitz constant cannot assign substantial probability to many well-separated modes. Covering many modes therefore requires either sharp transitions in base space or off-support bridge regions in action space. Experiments on synthetic multimodal tasks and robotic simulation benchmarks support these mechanisms.

### [145] [Lost in Tokenization: Fundamental Trade-offs in Graph Tokenization for Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22471)
*Maya Bechler-Speicher,Gilad Yehudai,Gil Harari,Clayton Sanford,Amir Globerson,Joan Bruna*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了图Transformer中“图标记化”对模型表达能力的影响，证明了不同的标记化方式（如光谱、随机游走）会导致计算效率和表达能力的显著差异，并强调了结合多种互补标记化方案的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图Transformer的性能高度依赖于图到标记（Graph-to-token）的映射方式，即图标记化（Tokenization）。现有研究缺乏对不同标记化策略如何影响Transformer表达能力和计算效率的系统性理论理解，因此本文旨在探究标记化选择对图学习模型表达能力的本质影响。

Method: 本文通过理论分析与实验验证相结合的方法：1. 对比分析了光谱（Spectral）、随机游走（Random-walk）和邻接矩阵（Adjacency）三种基础标记化方式；2. 从理论上证明了不同标记化诱导了不同的深度机制（Depth Regimes）；3. 建立了相关下界与不可能定理；4. 在合成数据集和真实世界任务上进行了受控实验，验证了各标记化方式的局限性及其互补性。

Result: 研究表明：1. 随机游走标记化在任何游走长度下都是有损的；2. 光谱标记化虽无损但对局部任务而言存在条件数差的问题；3. 有限深度的Transformer难以在不同的标记化族之间进行高效转换；4. 实验证明了不同任务对结构视角的偏好不同，结合多种标记化方式能产生互补效应。

Conclusion: 图标记化（Tokenization）是图Transformer的核心要素，不同的标记化方式会导致模型表达能力的本质差异。没有一种万能的标记化方案，通过融合多种互补的标记化方式，可以显著提升模型在各类图任务中的表现。

Abstract: Transformers have become a central architecture for graph learning, but their application to graphs requires first choosing a tokenization: a graph-to-token map that determines which structural information is exposed at the input. In this work, we show that this choice is a fundamental component of transformer expressivity. We examine three tokenizations that serve as building blocks for many existing graph tokenizations: spectral, random-walk, and adjacency tokenizations. We prove that different tokenizations induce distinct depth regimes: the same graph computation may be realizable by a shallow transformer under one tokenization, while requiring substantially larger depth under another. For example, we prove that random-walk tokenization is lossy for any walk length, making it impossible in general to recover the graph from it, and that while spectral tokenization is lossless, it is ill-conditioned for local tasks. We further show that although both random-walk and spectral tokenizations are derived from adjacency information, it is impossible for a limited-depth transformer to convert between tokenization families in general. In particular, we establish lower bounds and impossibility results showing that unfavorable tokenizations may preclude the efficient recovery of more suitable structural representations. Finally, we complement our theory with controlled experiments on synthetic and real-world tasks, validating the predicted separations and showing that different tasks favor different structural views, and combining complementary tokenizations allows the transformer to leverage distinct signals from each representation.

</details>


### [146] [Represented Is Not Computed: A Causal Test of Candidate Algorithmic Intermediates in a Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22488)
*Ishita Darade,Sushrut Thorat*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文通过算术任务对比了模型解释中的线性探针与因果分析方法，发现即使模型看似计算出了算法中间量，其实际运行的因果电路却并非如此，证明了仅凭探针结果推断算法机制存在局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究结构化提示（Structured prompts）的内部实现机制。由于语言或视觉任务中任务相关关系定义模糊，作者选择算术任务作为受控环境，旨在探究Transformer模型是否真的遵循类似人类的闭式解算法进行分步计算，并对比探针分析与因果分析的结论差异。

Method: 作者通过训练一个Transformer模型执行“基数提取任务”（即计算 $N$ 在 $B$ 进制下 $B^D$ 位的系数），并利用线性探针（Linear Probes）检测中间计算步骤，同时结合因果干预测试（Causal tests）和稀疏电路搜索（Sparse circuit search）来验证计算路径的真实性。

Result: 模型在任务上达到99.83%的准确率；线性探针能够成功解码出闭式解所需的中间量；然而，因果测试与电路搜索显示，模型实际使用的计算路径与探针暗示的分步处理逻辑不符，计算路由在后期才进行结合。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了线性探针（Linear probes）与因果分析（Causal tests）在解释模型内部机制时可能存在显著偏差。尽管模型表现出与算术闭式解一致的中间表征，但稀疏电路搜索表明，实际的计算路径并未直接传输这些中间结果，这警示我们在利用探针推断模型内部算法时需保持谨慎。

Abstract: Structured prompts require integrating components according to task-relevant relations. How a network implements this integration is often hard to judge in language or vision, where those relations are rarely specified precisely enough to define a candidate internal algorithm. Arithmetic offers a cleaner setting. We study a Transformer trained on base-digit extraction: given $N$, $B$, and $D$, it must report the coefficient of $B^D$ in the base-$B$ expansion of $N$. The closed-form solution, $\lfloor N/B^D \rfloor \bmod B$, provides explicit candidate algorithmic intermediates. Across three seeds, the model reaches 99.83% exact-answer accuracy on held-out number-base intersections, establishing reliable task competence. Linear probes decode the intermediates, making staged arithmetic computation plausible. Causal tests then separate representation from use: within the localized route from the stream with $D$ as input to the output positions, behavior depends on early $D$-selective communication, independent of $N$ and $B$. Relatedly, a sparse circuit search finds mostly separate $N$, $B$, and $D$ routes that combine late rather than the staged route suggested by the probes. Thus, the model represents the intermediates that make the closed-form solution plausible, but the identified localized causal route does not transmit them to the output stream. This case shows that probe-based conclusions can diverge sharply from causal observations, even when explicit algorithmic hypotheses are available.

</details>


### [147] [Abstraction for Offline Goal-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22711)
*Clarisse Wibault,Alexander Goldie,Antonio Villares,Maike Osborne,Jakob Foerster*

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种利用层级结构进行“绝对抽象”的方法，通过相对化选项和多层级表示，使强化学习智能体能在离线场景中有效复用跨状态空间的经验，从而提升学习效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现实世界的目标条件强化学习（GCRL）中，马尔可夫决策过程（MDPs）通常存在由于对称性和状态-目标对之间的共享结构所导致的显著冗余。现有的离线GCRL方法多关注通过时间抽象来缩短任务时域，缺乏对状态空间内冗余结构的有效抽象。

Method: 论文提出了将层级结构作为一种抽象机制（Absolute Abstraction），通过“相对化选项”（Relativised Options）和为不同层级设计独特的表示形式，使得智能体能够在相似的上下文语境中复用经验，并据此设计了两种学习相对化选项及抽象表征的算法。

Result: 实验结果表明，通过引入这种层级化和相对化的归纳偏置（Inductive Biases），智能体能够显著提升在离线GCRL任务中的表现，证明了该方法在处理复杂、冗余环境时的有效性。

Conclusion: 该论文证明了通过引入相对化选项和层级化的抽象表示，可以有效利用状态空间中的对称性和结构冗余，从而在离线目标条件强化学习中实现知识的泛化与复用，显著提升算法效率。

Abstract: Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) often exhibit significant redundancy due to symmetries and shared structure across state-goal pairs in real-world Goal-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (GCRL). While hierarchical policies have been motivated for horizon reduction via temporal abstraction in offline GCRL, we demonstrate that hierarchy also enables absolute abstraction. By introducing relativised options as well as distinct representations for different levels of the hierarchy, we demonstrate how an agent can reuse experience across similar contexts of the state-space. Based on this framework, we introduce two simple algorithms for learning relativised options and abstracting from the absolute frame of reference. Our experiments show that such inductive biases significantly improve performance in offline GCRL.

### [148] [The Signal in the Noise: OOD Detection Through Goodness-of-Fit Testing in Factorised Latent Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22496)
*Philipp Bomatter,Jack Geary,Henry Gouk*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于连续归一化流的OOD检测新方法——SITN，通过捕捉样本在映射空间中的非典型噪声特征，解决了传统生成模型似然估计不可靠及复杂性偏差的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的深度生成模型（尤其是基于似然的方法）在用于分布外（OOD）检测时，往往无法提供可靠的判别结果，且容易受到样本复杂性偏差（Complexity Bias）的影响，导致模型将复杂的OOD数据错误地判定为分布内数据。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为“噪声中的信号”（Signal in the Noise, SITN）的方法。该方法基于连续归一化流的质量守恒与微分同胚特性，通过分析样本映射到隐空间后的噪声分布特征（即OOD样本在先验分布中表现出高度异常的模式），实现单样本级别的OOD检测。

Result: 实验表明，SITN方法在多个标准基准数据集及合成扰动测试中表现优异，不仅有效缓解了传统似然方法的复杂性偏差问题，还在保持较低计算负担的同时，实现了对假阳性率的严格控制。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种无需OOD数据、计算开销小且能有效控制假阳性率的OOD检测方法，通过利用连续归一化流的微分同胚特性，成功克服了基于似然的方法在OOD检测中存在的复杂性偏差问题。

Abstract: Deep generative models offer a natural foundation for out-of-distribution (OOD) detection, yet prior work has shown that their assigned likelihoods are notoriously unreliable indicators for in- vs out-of-distribution data. In this paper, we address this problem by leveraging the diffeomorphic and mass-preserving properties of continuous normalising flows. Our analysis shows that OOD samples are mapped to noise samples that are highly atypical under the noise prior in ways not captured by the likelihood. Based on this observation, we propose a new method -- Signal in the Noise (SITN) -- for OOD detection on the single-sample level. SITN requires no access to OOD data, incurs minimal computational overhead, and provides strict control of false positive rates. Comprehensive evaluations through standard benchmarks and synthetic perturbations highlight the method's effectiveness and the absence of the complexity bias inherent to likelihood-based methods.

</details>


### [149] [The Value of Covariance Matching in Gaussian DDPMs and the Lanczos Sampler](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22723)
*Md Sahil Akhtar,Aymane El Gadarri,Vivek F. Farias,Adam D. Jozefiak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文解决了扩散模型因使用对角协方差导致的采样路径误差问题。作者提出通过匹配全协方差来将误差降至 O(1/T²)，并引入了无需训练且高效的 Lanczos 高斯采样器（LGS），仅需少量雅可比向量积即可实现高质量采样，显著提升了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的高斯扩散模型（DDPM）在处理反向过程时，使用各向同性对角协方差会导致路径 KL 散度存在 O(1/T) 的不可避免误差，这限制了模型在分类器引导等涉及轨迹扰动场景下的性能。

Method: 提出了 Lanczos 高斯采样器 (LGS)，这是一种无需训练且无需存储完整矩阵的方法，仅利用后验均值的雅可比向量积（JVP）计算协方差向量积，从而实现全协方差采样。

Result: LGS 算法的逼近误差随 Lanczos 步数呈指数级衰减。实验表明，仅需 3 个 Lanczos 步即可在多个图像基准测试中超越 OCM-DDPM 等强基准模型，证明了该方法在提升采样质量方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了匹配全协方差矩阵可以将路径KL散度从O(1/T)降低至O(1/T²)，并通过提出的 Lanczos 高斯采样器 (LGS) 证明了全协方差建模在实际应用中的可行性与高效性，为提升扩散模型的采样质量提供了新路径。

Abstract: A central error measure in Gaussian DDPMs is the path-space KL divergence between the exact reverse chain and the learned Gaussian reverse process. This quantity is especially relevant for procedures such as classifier guidance, which perturb the entire reverse trajectory rather than only the terminal sample. Prior analyses show that standard isotropic reverse covariances suffer an unavoidable $Ω(1/T)$ path-KL error as the number of denoising steps $T$ grows. We show that matching the full posterior covariance breaks this barrier, yielding an order-wise improvement that reduces the path KL to $O(1/T^2)$. To make full covariance matching practical, we introduce the Lanczos Gaussian sampler (LGS), a training-free, matrix-free method for sampling from the optimal reverse covariance using only covariance-vector products, which are available through Jacobian-vector products of the posterior mean. LGS avoids dense covariance storage and auxiliary covariance models. We prove that LGS approximation error decays exponentially in the number of Lanczos steps, where each Lanczos step requires a single Jacobian-vector product. Empirically, using only just three such steps improves sample quality over strong diagonal-covariance baselines, including OCM-DDPM, across standard image benchmarks. This identifies full covariance matching as both theoretically valuable and practically accessible for fast DDPM sampling.

### [150] [Generative Modeling by Value-Driven Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22507)
*Pablo Moreno-Muñoz,Adrian Müller,Gergely Neu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于随机控制的生成建模框架——价值驱动传输（VDT），通过线性规划方法实现了快速、直线的采样路径，并在保持高性能的同时兼容了现代生成模型的所有关键功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决现有生成模型（如基于流、扩散或薛定谔桥的模型）在传输路径曲率、采样效率以及算法鲁棒性方面的局限性，寻求一种既能保持高效计算，又能方便集成条件生成等高级特性的统一建模框架。

Method: 该研究将生成式建模问题重构为一个离散时间的线性规划问题，其对偶变量对应于最优值函数。研究人员开发了一种无仿真（simulation-free）的原始-对偶算法，用于求解近似最优值函数，并据此推导出生价值驱动传输（VDT）策略。

Result: 实验结果表明，VDT策略能够生成直线传输路径，从而实现更快速、稳定的采样，并在条件生成、无分类器引导及不成对数据转换等任务中展现出卓越的性能和良好的可扩展性。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的基于离散时间随机控制的VDT框架，为生成模型提供了一种高效、稳健且具有高度可扩展性的新范式，在实现直线传输路径的同时，保留并提升了扩散模型和流模型的灵活性。

Abstract: We propose a new framework for generative modeling based on a discrete-time stochastic control formulation of measure transport. Adapting classic results from control theory, we formulate our problem as a linear program whose dual variables correspond to the \emph{optimal value function} of the control problem, which directly encodes the optimal control policy. Exploiting this LP formulation, we develop an efficient simulation-free primal-dual algorithm for computing approximately optimal value functions and the associated \emph{value-driven transport} (VDT) policies which approximate the true optimal policy. We show that well-trained VDT policies enjoy numerous favorable properties in comparison with other state-of-the-art methods based on flows, diffusions, or Schrödinger bridges: they lead to straight transport paths which can be simulated quickly and robustly, and can be enhanced in all the same ways as diffusion and flow-based models (e.g., conditional generation, classifier-free guidance, unpaired data-to-data translation are all easy to incorporate). We evaluate our methodology in a range of experiments, with results that indicate strong performance and good potential for scalability.

### [151] [Disentanglement Beyond Generative Models with Riemannian ICA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22531)
*Edmond Cunningham*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了“黎曼独立成分分析（RICA）”，通过引入微分几何中的局部结构和解耦张量，成功在无需全局生成模型假设的情况下，从理论上解释了现代表征学习中的解耦现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的解耦理论（如ICA）严重依赖于全局生成模型假设，这与现代预训练编码器不依赖生成假设但仍表现出解耦性质的实践脱节，亟需一种不依赖全局生成模型的解耦理论。

Method: 引入黎曼ICA（RICA），将传统的全局生成模型替换为局部几何结构；提出了“解耦张量”，该张量结合了数据对数似然的黑塞矩阵（Hessian）和由模型诱导的里奇曲率（Ricci curvature）来衡量点对点解耦。

Result: 实验证明，在受控的源恢复设定中，RICA能够在多种流形上有效恢复潜在源，且其表现不依赖于观测数据的特定坐标表示，优于传统的ICA基准方法。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过黎曼几何框架可以将解耦从全局生成模型中解脱出来，利用局部几何结构（点对点解耦）来实现对潜在因子的恢复，为现代预训练表征学习的解耦特性提供了理论支持。

Abstract: There is a gap between the theoretical foundations of disentanglement and the practice of modern representation learning. Existing theoretical frameworks, particularly Independent Component Analysis (ICA) and its nonlinear variants, assume a generative model with statistically independent latent variables underlying the data so that disentanglement amounts to identifying the latents that could have generated the data. This generative framework is interpretable and theoretically justified, but its strong assumptions make it difficult to apply to modern representation learning. Modern pretrained encoders often learn features that exhibit disentangled properties without making generative assumptions, yet there is no general theory for interpreting these features as independent factors of variation. We take a step toward such a theory by introducing Riemannian ICA (RICA), which replaces ICA's global generative model with local geometric structure. RICA is founded on the observation that in ICA, the factors of variation underlying a data point can be understood through radial curves emanating from the point that map to axis-aligned lines in the latent space. We formalize this perspective using Riemannian geometry and introduce our theory in a way that is consistent with the existing generative approach. Our main contribution is the disentanglement tensor, which encodes a second-order notion of disentanglement that we call pointwise disentanglement. This tensor depends on the Hessian of the data log likelihood as well as the Ricci curvature induced by the model. In a controlled source recovery setting with known ground-truth sources, RICA recovers sources across several manifolds, while the success of ICA baselines depends on the coordinates used to represent the observations. Our work provides a theoretical basis for studying local disentanglement without assuming a global generative model.

</details>


### [152] [Relational Linear Properties in Language Models: An Empirical Investigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22532)
*Giovanni Valer,Luigi Gresele,Marco Bronzini,Emanuele Marconato*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于KL散度的探测方法，用于定量评估关系线性的强度。该方法相比传统的雅可比矩阵近似（如Hernandez等人提出的方法）更为高效且精确。通过该方法，研究者在四个数据集上跨不同层级和查询表述，考察了主语嵌入到宾语反嵌入的线性映射关系。

Result: 实验结果显示，关系线性在不同模型间存在差异，并呈现出与语言信息处理一致的层级规律。此外，查询语句的释义变更（Paraphrasing）会对线性属性的强度产生显著影响，证明了该属性对输入形式具有敏感性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，关系线性（Relational Linearity）在语言模型中并非普遍存在，其表现随模型架构、层级位置以及查询表述方式的变化而波动。这一发现对基于线性映射的知识提取方法提出了挑战，强调了模型内部知识存储复杂性对线性解释框架的制约。

Abstract: Linear properties are ubiquitous in the representations of language models; however, testing them experimentally remains a challenging task. This work focuses on relational linearity: the hypothesis that, for a fixed relation (e.g., "plays"), the unembedding of an object (e.g., "trumpet") can be predicted from the embedding of its subject (e.g.,"Miles Davis") by a linear map. We present an experimental method to test the formulation of relational linearity by Marconato et al. (2025). Specifically, we introduce a probing method, based on Kullback-Leibler divergence, to evaluate this property and examine its variation across layers and paraphrased relational queries. It is also more efficient than previous work; for example, it avoids the crude Jacobian approximations used in Linear Relational Embeddings by Hernandez et al. (2024). Our findings across four datasets show that relational linearity varies across models, exhibits layer-wise patterns consistent with prior observations about linguistic information in model representations, and is differently affected by changes in how the relation is phrased.

### [153] [F-TIS: Harnessing Diverse Models in Collaborative GRPO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22537)
*Nikolay Blagoev,Oğuzhan Ersoy,Wendelin Boehmer,Lydia Yiyu Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对大模型强化学习中异构模型协作导致的“离策略”样本收敛难题，提出了 F-TIS 训练范式，在保证通信效率的同时，实现了与同策略训练相当的收敛性并提升了模型泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 GRPO 等大模型强化学习训练方法通常依赖于同质化模型以保持“同策略”以保证收敛，但在实际的分布式系统中，不同算力与偏好的异构模型协作需求日益增加。解决异构协作带来的离策略数据对模型收敛的负面影响是本文的研究动力。

Method: 提出了过滤截断重要性采样（Filtered Truncated Importance Sampling, F-TIS）框架。该方法通过在强化学习训练中引入针对离策略样本的过滤与截断机制，有效地平衡了异构协作带来的通信效率与训练收敛稳定性。

Result: 实验表明，F-TIS 在多种异构设置下均能达到与纯同策略训练相同的收敛结果；在分布外任务（OOD）上，该方法表现出更强的泛化能力，模型性能提升最高可达 12%。

Conclusion: F-TIS 成功解决了异构模型参与强化学习训练时的离策略（off-policy）样本带来的收敛性难题。该方法不仅实现了与同策略（on-policy）训练相当的收敛效果，还在部分场景下展现了更好的泛化能力，为分布式、异构化的模型训练提供了高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning methods such as GRPO have seen great popularity in LLM post-training. In GRPO, models produce completions to a set of prompts, which are rewarded, and the policy is updated towards the relatively high reward completions. Due to the auto-regressive nature of models, the generation phase of such style of training can be extremely time consuming. As a solution, prior work has sought to distribute the inference step across many nodes, working parallel. These works assume primarily homogeneous models in the training in order to keep samples as close to on-policy as possible. This assumption may be impractical in decentralized systems, where parties with various computes and preferences may wish to collaborate on the same task. Thus, decentralized training requires an approach that can handle heterogeneous models - different models collaborating on the same tasks. However, this leads to highly off-policy samples presented during training, which prior work has identified that off-policy samples can hurt GRPO convergence. To enable heterogeneity, we propose Filtered Truncated Importance Sampling (F-TIS) - a GRPO-style training paradigm that can use off-policy samples to improve local model's learning. Our framework allows various models to collaborate in the same RL training run while being communication efficient. We extensively evaluate F-TIS in various heterogeneous setups and we show that it exhibits identical final model convergence to purely on-sample training. Furthermore, we observe in some setups better generalization on out-of-distribution tasks than on-policy training, increasing model's performance by up to 12\%.

### [154] [ImplicitTerrainV2: Wavelet-Guided Spatially Adaptive Neural Terrain Representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22556)
*Haoan Feng,Xin Xu,Leila De Floriani*

TL;DR: ImplicitTerrainV2通过小波引导的自适应架构和高效压缩技术，实现了地形的高精度、连续性隐式神经表示，在大幅提升精度和降低模型规模的同时，显著优化了训练效率。

Abstract: Digital elevation models (DEMs) underpin terrain analysis in Geographic Information Systems (GIS), but in their common raster form, they rely on interpolation for off-grid sampling and finite-difference operators for derivative-based analysis. Implicit neural representations (INRs) offer a continuous alternative, but prior terrain INRs lack explicit frequency control, neglect the gradient structure of terrain, and remain too large and costly to train for practical deployment. We present ImplicitTerrainV2, which advances terrain INRs toward a compact, efficient neural terrain data format by combining a spectral control mechanism with wavelet-guided spatial adaptivity, derivative-aware supervision, and post-training model compression. At its core, a wavelet complexity field (WCF) derives spatially-adaptive frequency masks from analytically computed wavelet coefficients, localizing high-frequency capacity to complex terrain regions. The same field guides complexity-aware adaptive sampling that concentrates training in high-complexity regions, while gradient matching applies extra supervision to enforce the smooth manifold structure of terrain DEMs for improved derivative fidelity. Post-training mixed-precision quantization and entropy coding reduce storage to 1.23 bpp with a 0.28 dB PSNR drop. On 50 Swiss terrain tiles, ImplicitTerrainV2 reaches 66.25 dB end-to-end PSNR, improving over the prior work by 5.70 dB while using 3.2x fewer parameters and training in 55 s per tile on a single GPU. Our compressed neural format is competitive with several established DEM codecs in rate-distortion performance, while additionally supporting off-grid point queries, closed-form derivative evaluation, and resolution-independent reconstruction, which may benefit many downstream GIS applications.

### [156] [Regret-Based $(ε,δ)$-optimal Stopping Criteria for Bayesian Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22561)
*Haowei Wang,Jingyi Wang,Qiyu Wei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对贝叶斯优化缺乏理论停止准则的问题，推导了GP-UCB算法更紧致的后悔界，并据此提出了一种能保证获得ε-最优解的理论停止准则，有效平衡了优化质量与评估成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的贝叶斯优化（BO）通常在预设的评估预算耗尽后终止，但这既可能导致不必要的成本浪费，也无法提供关于解质量的最优性保证。目前缺乏理论上完善的BO停止准则，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 1. 推导了GP-UCB在任意迭代次数下更紧致的瞬时后悔界（instantaneous regret bounds）；2. 基于该紧致界设计了新的停止准则，在保证获得ε-最优解的前提下，以高概率（1-δ）终止优化过程。

Result: 数值实验结果表明，该停止准则能够有效地在保证解的质量的前提下，通过适时终止评估来节省计算资源，证明了其在实际应用中的有效性和高效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于紧致后悔界（regret bound）的停止准则在理论上是可靠的，能够确保在满足预设精度ε和置信度1-δ的情况下终止BO过程，有效解决了以往BO在终止时缺乏理论最优性保证的问题。

Abstract: Bayesian optimization (BO) is a widely used iterative black-box optimization method that utilizes Gaussian process (GP) surrogate models. In practice, BO is typically terminated after a fixed evaluation budget is exhausted, which can incur unnecessary cost and provides no optimality guarantee on solution quality. Recent research in developing a practical stopping criterion has made empirical progress, yet a theoretically sound stopping criterion remains a work in progress. In this work, we present provably tighter instantaneous regret bounds for GP upper confidence bound (GP-UCB) at any given iteration. Then, we propose stopping criteria for GP-UCB based on this tighter bound that ensures an $ε$-optimal solution with high probability $1-δ$ upon termination. Numerical experiments are performed to validate and demonstrate the effectiveness and efficiency of our stopping criteria.

</details>


### [157] [SDPM: Survival Diffusion Probabilistic Model for Continuous-Time Survival Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22776)
*Stanislav R. Kirpichenko,Andrei V. Konstantinov,Lev V. Utkin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为SDPM的生存扩散概率模型，通过生成式建模实现连续时间生存分析，避免了参数假设和时间离散化带来的误差，并在多项基准测试中展现出卓越的预测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的生存分析方法往往对风险函数施加结构性假设，或对时间轴进行离散化，这不仅限制了模型的灵活性，还引入了近似误差。作者旨在开发一种无需参数假设且无需离散化的连续时间生成式模型。

Method: 提出了生存扩散概率模型（SDPM），通过去噪扩散模型对生存结果（观测时间与删失指标的联合分布）进行建模。采用标准化的对数时间转换和连续高斯混合表示删失指标，并利用生成的条件样本通过Kaplan-Meier估计器推导生存函数。

Result: 在十个真实生存数据集上的评估显示，SDPM在C-index、集成时间依赖AUC和集成Brier分数等指标上具有极强的竞争力；在合成数据实验中，SDPM能比基准模型更准确地恢复连续生存分布的形状。

Conclusion: SDPM是一种强大的生成式生存分析模型，通过扩散模型绕过了传统的参数假设和时间离散化限制。它在预测性能和恢复真实生存分布形状方面表现出色，证实了扩散概率模型在处理生存分析这一复杂回归任务中的有效性。

Abstract: Survival analysis aims to estimate a time-to-event distribution from data with censored observations. Many existing methods either impose structural assumptions on the hazard function or discretize the time axis, which may limit flexibility and introduce approximation errors. We propose the Survival Diffusion Probabilistic Model (SDPM), a generative approach to continuous-time survival analysis. SDPM models the conditional distribution of the survival outcome, represented by the pair of observed time and censoring indicator, $\mathbb{P}(T,δ\mid \mathbf{x})$, using a denoising diffusion model. Under the assumption of conditionally independent censoring, conditional samples generated by the model can be transformed into survival function estimates using the Kaplan-Meier estimator. This formulation avoids parametric assumptions on the event-time distribution and does not require a discretization of the output time space. The model operates in a transformed target space, using standardized log-times and a continuous Gaussian-mixture representation of the censoring indicator. We evaluate SDPM on ten real survival datasets and compare it with five strong baselines, including tree-based, boosting-based, and neural survival models. Results show that SDPM achieves competitive predictive performance across C-index, integrated time-dependent AUC, and integrated Brier score. A study on synthetic Cox-Weibull data demonstrates that SDPM can recover the shape of an underlying continuous survival distribution more accurately than a strong nonparametric baseline when sufficiently many samples are generated. An ablation study confirms the importance of the proposed target-space transformations, which improve event-rate calibration, reduce invalid generated times, and provide consistent gains in predictive discrimination. Codes implementing the proposed model are publicly available.

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents demonstrate strong reasoning and execution capabilities on complex tasks when guided by structured instructions, commonly referred to as workflows. However, existing workflow-assisted agent serving systems typically rely on predefined templates and shallow matching mechanisms, which limit their ability to capture deep semantic relationships and generalize to previously unseen tasks. To address these limitations, we propose a new workflow management paradigm that represents workflows using a unified graph, termed wGraph, where each node corresponds to an atomic operation. wGraph serves as a shared substrate from which task-specific workflows are dynamically instantiated. Building on wGraph primitives, we introduce GraphFlow, a system that efficiently integrates workflows into agent serving through two key designs. First, adaptive workflow generation dynamically constructs workflows from wGraph based on task semantics and constraint requirements. Second, workflow state management exploits wGraph structure to efficiently manage Key-Value (KV) caches, reducing redundant computation during agent serving. *Vishal Rajput*

Conclusion: 该论文揭示了鲁棒性、领域自适应和不变性等多种看似独立的问题，本质上都可以归结为对“标签保持的部署扰动协方差”的估计与正则化。通过匹配原则和雅可比矩阵正则化，该理论为设计更鲁棒的机器学习模型提供了统一的数学框架。

Abstract: Robustness, domain adaptation, photometric and occlusion invariance, compositional generalisation, temporal robustness, alignment safety, and classical anisotropic regularisation are usually treated as separate problems with separate method families. This paper argues that much of their shared structure is one statistical problem: estimate the covariance of label-preserving deployment nuisance, then regularise the encoder Jacobian along a matrix whose range covers that covariance (the matching principle). CORAL, adversarial training, IRM, augmentation, metric learning, Jacobian penalties, and alignment-style constraints are different estimators of that object, not independent robustness tricks.
  In the linear-Gaussian model we prove closed-form optimality (Theorem A), including cube-root water-filling within the matched range; necessity of range coverage for quadratic Jacobian penalties (Theorem G); the same range dichotomy at deep global minima; and two falsification controls (Lemma C; Corollaries E), with seven conditional consistency lemmas (D1-D7) for estimation under standard identifiability assumptions.
  We introduce the Trajectory Deviation Index (TDI), a label-free probe of embedding sensitivity when task accuracy or Jacobian Frobenius norm is insufficient.
  Thirteen pre-registered blocks from classical ML through Qwen2.5-7B test the predicted matched, then isotropic, then wrong-W ordering on geometry and deployment drift; twelve pass, and the sole exception (Office-31) is an eigengap failure named before the run. At 7B scale, matched style-PMH improves selective honesty and preserves Style TDI where standard DPO degrades it.
  The contribution is naming the deployment nuisance covariance, stating what the regulariser must do, and supplying a closed-form falsifiable theory once that object is identified, not universality on every leaderboard.

Method: 本文采用了平均场分析（mean-field analysis）方法，结合对数-索博列夫不等式（log-Sobolev inequalities），分析了WPO中梯度流的能量耗散特性，并证明了在满足特定正则性假设条件下，值函数能够线性收敛至全局最优解。

Abstract: Wasserstein Policy Optimization (WPO) is a recently proposed reinforcement learning algorithm that leverages Wasserstein gradient flows to optimize stochastic policies in continuous action spaces. Despite its empirical success, the theoretical convergence properties of WPO in environments with continuous state and action spaces have yet to be fully established. In this note, we argue that WPO within the framework of entropy-regularised Markov Decision Processes converges linearly. This is done by leveraging recent advances in mean-field analysis for convergence of gradient flows using log-Sobole inequalities. Assuming existence of sufficiently regular solution to the gradient flow equation we demonstrate monotonic energy dissipation along the flow and establish a local log-Sobolev inequality. Ultimately, these properties allow us to argue that the value function should converge linearly to the global optimum.

### [161] [Posterior Collapse as Automatic Spectral Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22691)
*Johannes Hirn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究发现β-VAE中的后验崩溃其实是一种自动化的特征剪枝过程。通过兰道稳定性分析，揭示了潜变量会根据其重构效用，遵循平均场定律依次发生级联式崩溃，从而为模型解释性和特征筛选提供了理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解释β-VAE中普遍存在的“后验崩溃”现象（即部分潜变量被忽视），并探究其背后的理论机制。研究人员希望理解这种崩溃过程是否具备某种可预测的结构化规律，以及如何利用这一特性进行模型分析。

Method: 1. 使用兰道稳定性分析（Landau stability analysis）对β-VAE的损失函数进行分析。
2. 定义了一个潜变量重缩放不变的序参量（order parameter）来对活跃的潜变量模式进行排序。
3. 在线性高斯假设下，对比崩溃谱、效用谱和归一化PCA谱，并推导了崩溃遵循的平均场定律。
4. 使用WorldClim数据集对上述理论预测进行了实证检验。

Result: 1. 证明了在β-VAE中，潜变量的崩溃是由β参数设定的重构贡献阈值决定的。
2. 在线性高斯模型下，确认了崩溃谱、效用谱与PCA谱的一致性，且崩溃现象遵循平均场定律。
3. 验证了β的增加会导致潜变量模式呈级联式（cascade）崩溃。

Conclusion: 论文得出结论，β-VAE的后验崩溃（posterior collapse）本质上是一种自动化的谱剪枝过程。通过兰道稳定性分析，该过程能够根据潜变量对重构的贡献大小，按照从“最不重要”到“最重要”的顺序依次发生崩溃，从而揭示了数据的层次化表示。

Abstract: We show that posterior collapse in $β$-VAEs implements automatic spectral pruning. A latent mode collapses if its contribution to reconstruction is below the cutoff set by $β$. Equilibrium solutions with different $β$ thus reveal a cascade of collapses as latent modes decouple from least to most useful.
  We derive this as a consequence of the loss via a Landau stability analysis. We define a latent-rescaling-invariant order parameter that ranks active latent modes and whose collapse thresholds identify which effective variables to inspect first.
  In the linear Gaussian case, the collapse spectrum, utility spectrum, and normalized PCA spectrum coincide, and each collapse follows a mean-field law. We test these predictions on the WorldClim dataset.

### [162] [Clipping Bottleneck: Stabilizing RLVR via Stochastic Recovery of Near-Boundary Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22703)
*Shuo Yang,Jinda Lu,Chiyu Ma,Kexin Huang,Haoming Meng,Qihui Zhang,Yuyang Liu,Bolin Ding,Guoyin Wang,Li Yuan,Jingren Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型强化学习（RLVR）中硬截断导致有效训练信号丢失的问题，本文提出了 NSR（Near-boundary Stochastic Rescue）方法，通过随机保留边界附近的信号，显著提升了模型训练的稳定性和最终性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对当前大规模语言模型（LLM）推理任务中广泛使用的强化学习（RLVR）范式，作者指出 GRPO 类算法中硬截断（Hard Clipping）机制会导致位于边界附近的有效信息被丢弃，从而引发训练不稳定和收敛次优的问题。

Method: 提出了“近边界随机救援”（Near-boundary Stochastic Rescue, NSR）方法。该方法在执行策略梯度更新时，对超出预设截断阈值的 token 进行随机保留（而非一律丢弃），从而在边界附近恢复重要的训练信号。该机制在数学上表现为隐式的梯度衰减，但其特定的局部随机救援机制优于传统的确定性梯度衰减。

Result: 在 7B 到 30B 参数规模的模型（包括稠密模型和 MoE 架构）上进行了广泛实验。结果表明，NSR 显著提升了训练稳定性，并优于 DAPO 和 GSPO 等现有基准模型，证明了该方法在提升 RLVR 训练效果方面的有效性和通用性。

Conclusion: NSR 是一种简单且高效的即插即用型改进方法，通过在边界附近引入随机性，解决了 GRPO 类算法中因硬截断而导致的信号丢失问题，显著提升了 LLM 在强化学习任务中的稳定性和收敛性能。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a central paradigm for scaling LLM reasoning, yet its optimization often suffers from training instability and suboptimal convergence. Through a systematic dissection of clipping-based GRPO-style objectives, we identify the rigid clipping decision induced by hard clipping as a key practical bottleneck in the studied RLVR setups. Specifically, our analysis suggests that informative signals can lie in the near-boundary region just beyond the clipping threshold, and are therefore discarded by the standard hard-clipping rule. Notably, once this bottleneck is precisely identified, even simple stochastic perturbations at the boundary can recover meaningful performance gains. Building on this finding, we propose Near-boundary Stochastic Rescue (NSR), a minimal, plug-and-play modification that stochastically retains these slightly out-of-bound tokens to recover lost signals. While NSR, via stochastic sampling, can be interpreted as inducing an implicit gradient decay in expectation, our ablations reveal that its stochastic, boundary-local rescue mechanism is consistently more effective than deterministic gradient decay. Validated by extensive experiments across model sizes from 7B to 30B and both dense and MoE architectures, as a plug-and-play solution, NSR substantially improves training stability and delivers consistent gains over strong baselines such as DAPO and GSPO.
