### [199] [IdleSpec: Exploiting Idle Time via Speculative Planning for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22154)
*Daewon Choi,Kyunghyun Park,Woomin Song,Saket Dingliwal,Sai Muralidhar Jayanthi,Jinwoo Shin,Aram Galstyan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: IdleSpec 是一种通过利用 LLM 智能体在等待工具调用反馈时的“空闲时间”进行并行推理规划的方法，通过学习策略采样动态生成规划候选项，显著提高了智能体在复杂、长时程任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM 智能体在执行多步任务时，频繁与外部工具交互会导致显著的“空闲等待时间”。现有的工作要么将此视为不可避免的损耗，要么方案过于局限，未能充分考虑不同工具调用的计算预算差异及未来观测的不确定性，从而导致算力浪费和智能体性能受限。

Method: IdleSpec 核心方法包括：1. 空闲时间规划：在等待环境反馈的间隙，利用计算资源迭代生成规划候选项；2. 策略采样：根据习得的分布，在“进度规划”（progressive）和“恢复规划”（recovery）两种互补策略间进行采样，以应对环境观测的不确定性；3. 聚合机制：当观测结果到达时，将生成的规划候选项与观测数据聚合，指导后续的推理步骤。

Result: 实验表明，IdleSpec 显著提升了智能体在多个场景下的性能：在 GAIA 和 FRAMES 基准上，使用 Gemini-2.5-Flash 时准确率达到 55.6%，较基线提升 5.1%；在涉及大量代码执行延时的 MLE-Bench 上，Any Medal 率提升高达 9.1%。

Conclusion: IdleSpec 提出了一种通用的推断范式，通过有效利用智能体在工具调用等待期间的空闲时间进行推理规划，显著提升了复杂任务处理的准确性，并验证了该方法在多种长时程任务基准上的鲁棒性和普适性。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based agents solve complex tasks by leveraging multi-step reasoning with iterative tool calls and environment interactions, which incur idle time while waiting for observations. Despite the prevalence of idle time in most agentic scenarios, existing works treat it as an unavoidable overhead or propose restricted solutions that overlook varying computational budgets across different tool calls and future observation uncertainty, thereby leading to suboptimal utilization of idle time. In this paper, we introduce IdleSpec, a scalable and generic inference approach that leverages idle-time computation to improve agent performance while minimizing latency overhead. Specifically, IdleSpec iteratively generates plan candidates during idle periods and, once observations become available, aggregates them to guide the next reasoning step. For effective plan generation under observation uncertainty, IdleSpec samples between complementary drafting strategies (i.e., progressive and recovery) from a learned distribution that is updated via posterior feedback. Our experiments demonstrate that IdleSpec significantly improves agent performance in various agentic scenarios by effectively utilizing idle time. In particular, on the GAIA and FRAMES, IdleSpec achieves 55.6% average accuracy with Gemini-2.5-Flash, surpassing the vanilla baseline without idle-time usage by 5.1%. Furthermore, for MLE-Bench, which involves substantial delay from code executions, IdleSpec achieves performance gains of up to 9.1% on the Any Medal rate, highlighting its generalizability to long-horizon tasks.

</details>


### [200] [ST-SimDiff: Balancing Spatiotemporal Similarity and Difference for Efficient Video Understanding with MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22158)
*Bingjun Luo,Tony Wang,Chaoqi Chen,Xinpeng Ding*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对多模态大模型处理长视频计算开销大的问题，提出了一种名为 ST-SimDiff 的免训练框架，通过时空图建模结合“相似性去冗余”与“差异性捕获关键事件”的策略，有效平衡了计算效率与信息留存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频理解方法在处理长视频时，因视觉 token 数量巨大导致计算开销过高，且现有剪枝或合并方案往往忽略了视频中关键的变化点和转折点，缺乏对时空关联的协同建模能力。

Method: 提出了一种免训练的框架 ST-SimDiff：首先将视频视觉 token 构建为时空图以统一建模关联性；其次采用双重选择策略：一是基于相似性的社区检测，压缩冗余的静态信息；二是基于时序差异的选择，定位并保留关键的动态变化点。

Result: 实验结果表明，ST-SimDiff 在显著降低计算成本的同时，在多个基准测试中超越了现有的先进方法，证明了其在捕捉长视频关键动态特征方面的有效性。

Conclusion: ST-SimDiff 通过时空图建模和“相似性去冗余、差异性捕获关键”的双重策略，成功实现了在极低算力开销下对长视频内容的高效表征，证明了在无需额外训练的情况下，通过精细化的视觉特征筛选能够显著提升多模态大模型的推理性能。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) face significant computational overhead when processing long videos due to the massive number of visual tokens required. To improve efficiency, existing methods primarily reduce redundancy by pruning or merging tokens based on importance or similarity. However, these approaches largely overlook a critical dimension of video content, i.e., changes and turning points, and they lack a collaborative model for spatio-temporal relationships. To address this, we propose a new perspective: similarity is for identifying redundancy, while difference is for capturing key events. Based on this, we designed a training-free framework named ST-SimDiff. We first construct a spatio-temporal graph from the visual tokens to uniformly model their complex associations. Subsequently, we employ a parallel dual-selection strategy: 1) similarity-based selection uses community detection to retain representative tokens, compressing static information; 2) temporal difference-based selection precisely locates content-changing points to preserve tokens that capture key dynamic shifts. This allows it to preserve both static and dynamic content with a minimal number of tokens. Extensive experiments show our method significantly outperforms state-of-the-art approaches while substantially reducing computational costs. Our code is available in https://github.com/bingjunluo/ST-SimDiff.

</details>


### [201] [Adapting the Interface, Not the Model: Runtime Harness Adaptation for Deterministic LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22166)
*Tianshi Xu,Huifeng Wen,Meng Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对大模型智能体在确定性环境中因“接口不匹配”导致的交互失败，本文提出了 Life-Harness。该方法在不改变模型权重的前提下，通过优化运行时接口与交互逻辑，实现了智能体性能的大幅提升与跨模型的可迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的智能体适配方法主要集中在更新模型参数上，但在确定性、规则导向的领域中，许多失败的根源在于大模型与环境接口之间的不匹配，而非模型能力本身不足。因此，研究人员希望通过优化运行环境机制来弥补这一缺陷。

Method: 提出了 Life-Harness，这是一个生命周期感知的运行时框架。该方法通过分析训练轨迹，将反复出现的交互失败转化为可复用的干预措施，涵盖了环境契约（environment contracts）、程序技能（procedural skills）、动作实现（action realization）和轨迹控制（trajectory regulation）四个维度，并在测试阶段保持固定，无需修改大模型权重。

Result: 在包含 τ-bench、τ²-bench 和 AgentBench 的七个确定性环境中，Life-Harness 在 126 个模型-环境设置中的 116 个取得了性能提升，平均相对改进率达 88.5%。此外，仅基于单个模型（Qwen3-4B-Instruct）训练的框架成功迁移至其他 17 个模型，证明了其捕获的是环境层面的通用结构。

Conclusion: 本文证明了在不调整模型权重的情况下，通过改进“运行时环境（Runtime Harness）”来提升大模型智能体表现是高度有效的。生命周期感知的运行时框架不仅能解决模型与环境接口不匹配的问题，还具备跨模型的可迁移性，为智能体进化提供了一种比模型训练更轻量、更高效的补充方案。

Abstract: LLM agents are shaped not only by their language models, but also by the runtime harness that mediates observation, tool use, action execution, feedback interpretation, and trajectory control. While existing agent adaptation methods mainly update model parameters, many failures in deterministic, rule-governed domains stem from mismatches at the model--environment interface. We propose Life-Harness, a lifecycle-aware runtime harness that improves frozen LLM agents without changing model weights or evaluation environments. Life-Harness evolves from training trajectories by converting recurring interaction failures into reusable interventions across environment contracts, procedural skills, action realization, and trajectory regulation, and remains fixed during held-out evaluation. On seven deterministic environments from $τ$-bench, $τ^2$-bench, and AgentBench, Life-Harness improves 116 out of 126 model--environment settings across 18 model backbones, with an average relative improvement of 88.5%. Harnesses evolved only from Qwen3-4B-Instruct trajectories transfer to 17 other models, showing that Life-Harness captures reusable environment-side structure rather than model-specific behavior. These results position runtime interface adaptation as a complementary alternative to model-centric agent training. Code is available at GitHub.

### [202] [Measuring Cross-Modal Synergy: A Benchmark for VLM Explainability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22168)
*Joël Roman Ky,Salah Ghamizi,Maxime Cordy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了评估VLM跨模态推理的现有指标失效问题，并提出了全新的“协同忠实度”指标，该指标能有效区分真实的跨模态逻辑与伪造的视觉显著性，为VLM的可解释性评估提供了更科学的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的VLM解释方法多依赖单模态扰动指标，但由于多模态数据中存在语言先验和模态偏差，模型往往能仅凭文本就回答视觉查询。这导致单模态指标会错误地惩罚忠实解释者，造成评估范式的崩塌。

Method: 作者提出了一种基于Shapley交互索引（Shapley Interaction Index）的评估指标——协同忠实度（Synergistic Faithfulness, F_syn）。该方法通过严格隔离模态间的联合Harsanyi红利，有效解耦了视觉合理性与跨模态忠实度，并实现了显著的计算加速。

Result: F_syn指标在预测准确度上达到了0.92的相关性，且计算速度提升了24倍。实验表明，现有的XAI方法在捕捉跨模态协同作用方面表现不佳，远不如经过调整的基于注意力的解释方法。此外，文中揭示了视觉排名的评价标准与跨模态忠实度存在本质矛盾。

Conclusion: 该研究指出，现有的视觉-语言模型（VLM）解释方法过度依赖视觉显著性，而忽视了模态间的协同作用。通过提出协同忠实度指标（F_syn），该工作为审计高风险部署下的VLM推理提供了更严谨的评估框架，纠正了以往评价范式的偏差。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) map complex visual inputs to semantic spaces, but interpreting the cross-modal reasoning of VLMs currently relies on post-hoc explainers evaluated via unimodal perturbation metrics. We expose a limitation in this paradigm: because multimodal datasets contain language priors and modality biases, VLMs frequently exhibit cross-modal redundancy, allowing them to answer visual queries using text alone. Consequently, unimodal metrics penalize faithful explainers, triggering an evaluation collapse where visual and textual rankings fundamentally contradict each other. %(Kendall's $τ= -0.06$). To resolve this, we introduce Synergistic Faithfulness ($\mathcal{F}_{syn}$), a scalable metric rooted in the Shapley Interaction Index that strictly isolates the joint Harsanyi dividend between modalities, serving as a highly accurate surrogate ($ρ= 0.92$) while achieving a $24\times$ computational speedup. Evaluating 8 distinct XAI methods across 3 VLM architectures and 3 benchmark datasets, reveals that explainers proposed for VLMs heavily over-index on visual salience and significantly underperform adapted attention-based methods in capturing true cross-modal synergy. By decoupling visual plausibility from cross-modal faithfulness, this work provides a rigorous evaluation framework required to safely audit VLM reasoning in high-stakes deployments.

### [203] [LLM-Metrics: Measuring Research Impact Through Large Language Model Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22176)
*Si Shen,Wenhua Zhao,Danhao Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种利用大语言模型参数化记忆评估科研影响力的新方法（LLM-Metrics），通过测试发现模型对高影响力论文有更强的记忆，为研究评估提供了一种实时、客观且独立于引用计数的新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对传统引用计数指标在评估科研影响力时存在的滞后性、学科偏见和马太效应等局限性，探索一种新的基于大模型参数化记忆的评估方法。

Method: 提出了“LLM-Metrics”，通过设计标题识别、作者识别、方法识别和会议识别四类多项选择题，利用大模型的参数化记忆对549篇计算机科学论文进行评估，并将其与引用计数进行对比分析。

Result: 实验显示，在17个被测模型中，15个产生了正相关预测（9个具有统计学显著性），整体Spearman相关系数为0.1495。特别是在2024年的论文中预测信号更强，且模型规模与预测能力呈现非单调关系，证明了该方法能够有效捕捉学术影响力且具备抗反向因果的能力。

Conclusion: LLM-Metrics 提供了一种实时、跨学科且独立于引用的新型研究影响力评估范式，证明了利用大模型的参数化记忆可以有效捕捉研究影响力。

Abstract: Citation counts remain the dominant metric for assessing research impact, yet they suffer from well-documented limitations: temporal lag, disciplinary bias, and Matthew effects. Here we propose LLM-Metrics, a research-impact assessment metric derived from the parametric memory of large language models (LLMs). The central hypothesis is that high-impact papers receive greater exposure in the academic community, that this exposure enters LLM training data in textual form, and that models consequently form stronger parametric memory of these papers. We designed four types of multiple-choice probes, covering title recognition, author recognition, method recognition, and venue recognition, and evaluated 549 computer science papers published in 2023-2024 across 17 LLMs spanning 0.5B to 72B parameters from six vendors. Of the 17 models, 15 produced positive predictions, 9 of which were significant at p less than 0.05, with an overall Spearman correlation of rho = 0.1495 and p = 0.0004 against citation counts. Three additional findings support the proposed mechanism. First, the predictive signal was stronger for 2024 papers, rho = 0.1880, whose citation counts were near zero at model-training time, reducing the plausibility of a simple reverse-causality explanation. Second, author-recognition probes showed the strongest discriminative power, consistent with an exposure-driven memory mechanism. Third, model scale and predictive power were non-monotonic: a 3B-parameter model, Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct, with rho = 0.1829, outperformed most larger models, supporting a selective-memory hypothesis in which the limited capacity of smaller models can serve as an effective information filter. LLM-Metrics offers a real-time, cross-disciplinary, citation-independent paradigm for research assessment.

### [204] [Skill Weaving: Efficient LLM Improvement via Modular Skillpacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22205)
*Zhuo Li,Guodong Du,Zesheng Shi,Weiyang Guo,Weijun Yao,Yuan Zhou,Jiabo Zhang,Jing Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SkillWeave 是一种通过模块化“技能包”和高效压缩技术来优化 LLM 的框架，实现了在极低资源占用下超越更大规模单体模型的多领域性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的方法难以在多领域能力与严格的内存及推理限制之间取得平衡，大型语言模型在特定领域应用时面临资源开销过大的挑战。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SkillWeave 的模块化框架，将通用模型的能力划分为“技能包”（Skillpacks，即轻量级的特定领域增量模块）；同时引入 SkillZip 技术对这些技能包进行压缩，使其具备紧凑的格式，从而在保持多领域性能的同时显著降低推理延迟。

Result: 在多任务和智能体基准测试中，9B 参数的 SkillWeave 模型性能超过了多个基准模型，甚至优于 32B 的单体 LLM，同时推理速度最高提升了 4 倍。

Conclusion: SkillWeave 证明了通过模块化架构和高效压缩技术，可以在严格的内存和算力预算下，实现超越传统大型单体模型的多领域专业化性能，为资源受限环境下的 LLM 部署提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly require specialization across diverse domains, yet existing approaches struggle to balance multi-domain capacities with strict memory and inference constraints. In this work, we introduce SkillWeave, a modular improvement framework that enables LLMs to specialize under fixed memory budgets. SkillWeave partitions full capabilities of a general-purpose model into skillpacks -- lightweight, domain-specific delta modules -- that reorganize and refine the model's internal knowledge. For efficient deployment, SkillWeave integrates SkillZip to compress skillpacks into compact and inference-ready format, enabling strong multi-domain performance with low-latency execution. On multi-task and agentic benchmarks, a 9B SkillWeave model outperforms several baselines and even surpasses a 32B monolithic LLM, while achieving up to 4x speedup.

### [205] [CLORE: Content-Level Optimization for Reasoning Efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22211)
*Yuyang Wu,Qiyao Xue,Guanxing Lu,Weichen Liu,Zihan Wang,Manling Li,Olexandr Isayev*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CLORE是一个通过优化推理内容（而非单纯限制长度）来提升大模型推理效率的训练框架，它通过自动编辑高质量的推理轨迹并进行对比学习，实现了更简洁、准确的思维链生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习后训练虽然提升了大模型的推理能力，但往往产生过长、重复或语义模糊的思维链。现有方法多侧重于长度约束，缺乏对中间推理内容的细粒度监督。

Method: 提出了一种名为CLORE的内容级优化框架。该方法利用外部增强模型对正确的推理轨迹进行局部编辑（删除重复、无关或冗余内容），保留正确答案；随后将原始与编辑后的轨迹对作为样本，结合辅助的无参考DPO目标和标准的策略梯度（如GRPO）进行训练，以减小分布偏移。

Result: 在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-7B和Qwen2.5-Math-7B上的实验表明，CLORE显著优化了准确性与效率之间的平衡，有效减少了重复推理、晦涩内容和答案后的无效探索，并与多种现有强化学习方法保持良好兼容。

Conclusion: CLORE证明了内容级监督是长度级控制的有效补充，能够通过精简思维链提升大模型的推理效率与准确性，且具有良好的兼容性。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning post-training has improved the reasoning ability of large language models, but often produces unnecessarily long, repetitive, or semantically opaque reasoning traces. Existing efficient reasoning methods mainly regulate response length through explicit budgets or length-aware rewards, leaving intermediate reasoning content weakly supervised. We propose CLORE, a content-level optimization framework that improves reasoning efficiency by editing correct on-policy rollouts. CLORE uses an external augmentation model to delete repetitive segments, illegible or task-irrelevant content, and superfluous reasoning after the solution is established, while preserving the final answer. The resulting augmented--original pairs are optimized with an auxiliary reference-free DPO objective alongside standard policy-gradient training. By restricting augmentation to correct trajectories and performing local deletion, CLORE keeps edited rollouts close to the policy distribution and mitigates off-policy mismatch. Experiments on DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-7B and Qwen2.5-Math-7B across five mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that CLORE improves the accuracy--efficiency trade-off and remains compatible with GRPO, DAPO, Training Efficient, and ThinkPrune. Content-level analyses further show that CLORE reduces repetitive reasoning, illegible content, and post-answer exploration, supporting content-level supervision as a complementary direction to length-level control.

### [206] [SGR-Bench: Benchmarking Search Agents on State-Gated Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22219)
*Ningyuan Li,Haiyang Shen,Mugeng Liu,Yudong Han,Zhuofan Shi,Sixiong Xie,Yun Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 SGR-Bench 基准，专门用于评估智能体在需要复杂状态配置（如多级过滤器）的专业网站中进行检索的能力。研究发现，即使是顶尖的智能体也难以应对此类任务，其核心瓶颈在于无法正确设置和保持检索状态，而非答案生成的错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的网页检索基准往往忽略了“状态受限检索”（State-gated retrieval, SGR）这一关键挑战。在许多专业数据网站中，获取证据不仅需要定位网页，还必须通过配置复杂的过滤器、视图或层级来实现特定的检索状态。目前的智能体在处理此类任务时表现尚不明晰，因此需要一个专门的基准来量化这一能力。

Method: 提出了 SGR-Bench 评估基准，包含 100 个专家策划的跨 6 类来源和 12 个数据生态系统的任务。这些任务通过“约束引导”和“目标导向”两种模式设计，以测试智能体在处理需配置特定检索状态（如过滤器、层级选择）的场景下的表现。研究评估了 8 种基于 CLI 的智能体系统和 3 种商业搜索智能体，并对失败案例进行了人工审计。

Result: 在 SGR-Bench 上，性能最强的系统仅达到 66.18% 的项目级 F1 分数，行级 F1 分数更低。通过对 156 个失败轨迹的审计发现，主要问题在于智能体无法正确建立检索状态：检索范围漂移（37.2%）和准则不匹配（27.6%）是失败的主要原因，而最终答案组成部分的错误仅占 10.3%。

Conclusion: 当前的智能体在处理需要复杂状态配置的专业检索任务时表现不佳，主要瓶颈在于无法正确建立和维护网站特定的检索状态（如过滤器、视图等），而非信息提取或答案生成能力。SGR-Bench 为未来研究如何提升智能体的环境交互与状态管理能力提供了标准化的评估平台。

Abstract: Recent advances in large language models and tool-using agents have expanded the range of benchmarked web tasks. Yet an important class of specialized retrieval tasks remains undercharacterized. On many specialized data-retrieval websites, answer-bearing evidence becomes accessible only after establishing the correct site-specific retrieval state through filters, views, hierarchies, or scopes. We term this capability state-gated retrieval (SGR). We introduce SGR-Bench, a benchmark for this setting containing 100 expert-curated tasks spanning six source families and 12 public data ecosystems. Each task requires discovering the appropriate website and configuring its site-specific retrieval state to produce a structured answer. SGR-Bench pairs constraint-guided and goal-oriented formulations of the same underlying problems, enabling controlled comparisons between explicit and implicit guidance for state-gated retrieval. We evaluate eight CLI-based agentic LLM systems and three commercial search-agent products. On SGR-Bench, the strongest system reaches only 66.18% item-level F1, while row-level F1 remains much lower. A manual audit of 156 analyzable failed CLI trajectories shows why: agents often reach a relevant web source, but establish the wrong site-specific retrieval state. Retrieval-scope drift (37.2%) and criterion mismatch (27.6%) dominate, whereas final answer composition accounts for only 10.3%. The dataset and single-case evaluation instructions are available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/PKUAIWeb/SGR-BENCH.

### [207] [Evaluating Large Language Models as Live Strategic Agents: Provider Performance, Hybrid Decomposition, and Operational Gaps in Timed Risk Play](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22238)
*H. C. Ekne*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究指出，大模型的实际效能远超静态基准测试的范畴。实验表明，端到端系统性能的差异主要源于模型在真实工作流中的执行力与目标导向行为，而非单纯的规划能力。因此，评估大模型应转向考察其作为系统组件在复杂任务中的综合表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态基准测试无法完全反映大语言模型在实际应用场景（即嵌入在重复循环、时间限制等复杂系统环境）中的行为表现，因此有必要研究模型在真实、动态受限工作流中的性能。

Method: 研究者构建了一个包含时间限制、格式约束和失效模式的定时多阶段“风险”（Risk）游戏环境，组织了跨供应商模型冠军赛。通过固定规则和执行支架（Gemini Flash）进行对比实验，分析了模型的规划能力与端到端系统行为之间的差异，并深入审查了模型在游戏过程中的计划与执行追踪记录。

Result: 在端到端比赛中，Gemini-3.1-pro-preview表现出显著优势（胜率较高）；但在标准化执行环境（排除执行差异）下，各模型规划能力趋于一致。分析显示，Gemini的优势主要源于其更强的目标追踪能力（更频繁地关注最终目标）及更高的执行转化效率（深层征服链的构建）。

Conclusion: 大语言模型的真实性能不仅取决于其规划能力，更受限于其在受限工作流中目标追踪、执行转换、成本控制及运行时可靠性的综合表现。因此，应将大模型视为有界工作流中的组件进行评估，而非仅作为孤立的基准测试响应者。

Abstract: Static benchmarks capture only part of how large language models behave in practice. Real systems place models inside repeated loops with time limits, formatting constraints, and failure modes. We study this setting in a timed multi-phase Risk environment with explicit victory targets and repeated planning and execution cycles. In a replicated 32-game cross-provider championship under frozen rules, gemini-3.1-pro-preview won 20 of 32 games against gpt-5.1, claude-opus-4-7, and kimi-k2.6, and the pooled winner distribution differs strongly from an equal-strength null (p approx 1.5 x 10^-5). We then separate planning from execution by standardizing execution on a cheaper Gemini Flash scaffold. Under this design, a pooled 32-game planner bakeoff is consistent with near-equality (p approx 0.821), which indicates that much of the earlier provider spread came from end-to-end system behavior rather than planning alone. To study mechanism, we analyze saved planning and execution traces from the provider championship. Gemini refers to the terminal objective far more often than the other models and increases that focus as victory approaches. Gemini also converts more turns into deep conquest chains, even though it is not the cleanest runtime. These results show that live-agent performance depends on objective tracking, execution conversion, cost, and runtime reliability, and they support evaluating LLMs as components in bounded workflows rather than as isolated benchmark respondents.

</details>

Yet post-trained LLMs are inherently conservative, and reward-shaping RL (e.g., GRPO) struggles since it only re-weights what an already passive policy samples. We show that conditioning on the user's latent concerns unlocks proactive capability that no amount of sampling can undermine, establishing these concerns as a pivotal training-time signal. To operationalize this finding, we build the \textbf{Cognitive User Simulator}, which models each user as a stratified persona comprising observable external traits and hidden internal concerns. The simulator produces faithful and diverse interactions, while emitting per-turn state dynamics that track persuasion progress. We then introduce \textbf{Simulator-Induced Asymmetric-View Policy Optimization}, which converts the modeled concerns and the simulation state transition into complementary training objectives: (1) \emph{Asymmetric On-Policy Self-Distillation} that transfers concern-aware behavior from a privileged view of the same policy into its deployable, conversation-only view; and (2) \emph{State-Transition Policy Refinement} ...

### [209] [SciCore-Mol: Augmenting Large Language Models with Pluggable Molecular Cognition Modules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22287)
*Yuxuan Chen,Changwei Lv,Yunduo Xiao,Zhongjing Du,Daquan Zhou,Yukun Yan,Zheni Zeng,Zhiyuan Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在处理分子、化学反应等异构科学数据时，面临离散符号与连续/拓扑数据之间的鸿沟，导致严重的语义缺失与噪声问题。

Method: 提出 SciCore-Mol 框架，包含三个深度集成的认知模块：1) 拓扑感知模块；2) 基于潜在扩散的分子生成模块；3) 反应感知推理模块。这些模块通过学习得到的表示接口与 LLM 主干耦合，从而超越了传统文本反馈的交互方式。

Result: SciCore-Mol 在分子理解、生成、反应预测及通用化学知识任务中表现优异。其 8B 参数系统在多项任务中达到或超过了商业闭源大模型的性能。

Conclusion: SciCore-Mol 通过模块化设计为大模型赋能科学领域提供了系统性的蓝图，证明了解耦、可插拔且灵活调度的模块是提升模型科学推理能力的有效路径，对药物研发及材料科学等领域具有重要意义。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are central to the one-for-all intelligent paradigm, but they face a fundamental challenge when dealing with heterogeneous scientific data such as molecules: the inherent gap between discrete linguistic symbols and topological molecular or continuous reaction data leads to significant information loss and semantic noise in text-based reasoning. We propose SciCore-Mol, a modular framework that bridges this gap through three deeply integrated pluggable cognitive modules: a topology-aware perception module, a latent diffusion-based molecular generation module, and a reaction-aware reasoning module. Each module is coupled to the LLM backbone through learned representation interfaces, enabling richer information exchange than is possible with text-only tool feedback. Our experiments on diverse chemical tasks demonstrate that SciCore-Mol achieves strong comprehensive performance across molecular understanding, generation, reaction prediction, and general chemistry knowledge, with an 8B-parameter open-source system that is competitive with and in several dimensions surpasses proprietary large models. This work provides a systematic blueprint for equipping LLMs with scientific expertise through decoupled, pluggable, and flexibly orchestrated modules, with direct implications for drug design, chemical synthesis, and broader scientific discovery.

### [210] [Cross-domain benchmarks reveal when coordinated AI agents improve scientific inference from partial evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22300)
*Fiona Y. Wong,Markus J. Buehler*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过四个跨学科基准测试评估了AI智能体协同在科学任务中的价值，发现其作用取决于任务类型：在多信号融合、增强可解释性或改进表征方面具有价值，但并非在所有场景下都能超越简单的科学工作流基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学证据通常分散在不同的仪器、数据库和学科中，单一来源难以覆盖完整现象。因此，亟需明确在何种科学任务中，多智能体协同系统相较于简单的科学工作流能够提供真正的增值价值，而非仅仅是复杂性的堆砌。

Method: 构建了一个涵盖四个科学领域（分子结构音乐化、范式转移检测、病媒疾病演化、系外行星筛选）的跨学科基准测试（ScienceClaw x Infinite）。通过设立固定的评估面板、预定义的评分协议、明确的基线模型以及消融实验，对AI智能体协同工作流与简单基线进行量化对比。

Result: 研究定义了三种智能体运作机制：1. 多源跨领域信息融合能提升任务性能（如疾病监测和行星筛选）；2. 在存在主导信号的场景下，协同主要提升了系统的可解释性和可溯源性（如范式转移检测）；3. 在某些情况下，协同带来的主要是表征层面的改善，而非预测性能的提升（如分子音乐化）。部分任务表明，简单的综合总结基线即可达到与复杂系统相当的性能。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，协调AI智能体在科学工作流中的价值并非普适的，而是高度依赖于任务场景。只有当跨领域数据融合能够带来性能提升、增强可解释性或提供更好的表征时，这种复杂系统才具有明确的优势。研究强调了在评估科学AI工具时，必须通过显式的对照组和评估面板来验证其真实贡献，而非默认协调系统优于简单基线。

Abstract: Scientific evidence often spans instruments, databases, and disciplines, so no single source records the full phenomenon. This makes it difficult to determine when coordinated AI agents add value over simpler scientific workflows. We evaluate this question with a cross-domain benchmark spanning four scientific tasks: mapping molecular structure into musical representations, detecting historical paradigm shifts in science, identifying vector-borne disease emergence, and vetting transiting-exoplanet candidates. Each case uses a frozen evaluation panel, predefined scoring protocols, explicit baselines, ablations or null controls, and stated limitations. The results define three operating regimes. When different disciplines each capture only part of the phenomenon, cross-channel composites improve over single-channel baselines: climate-vector emergence reaches AUROC 0.944 and exoplanet vetting reaches AUROC 0.955. However, the exoplanet workflow is effectively tied with a strong combined-summary baseline, showing that decomposition does not always improve top-line performance. When one signal dominates, as in paradigm-shift detection, coordination mainly improves interpretation and traceability. For molecular sonification, the gain is representational rather than predictive. ScienceClaw x Infinite provides the auditable artifact and provenance layer for this evaluation. The benchmark therefore assigns value to coordination only when the corresponding performance, provenance, or representation claim is supported by explicit comparators.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了名为 KGI-Bench 的基准测试框架，利用三个互补的质量指标（覆盖率、正确性和一致性）来评估输出的知识图谱，并提供了电影领域的基准数据集（包括种子知识图谱、不同格式的重叠输入数据以及作为真实值的参考知识图谱）。通过该框架，作者对比评估了 12 条不同的集成流水线。

Result: 通过对 12 条集成流水线的对比评估，研究验证了 KGI-Bench 在不同输入数据格式和设计选择下评估流水线行为的有效性和实用性。

Conclusion: KGI-Bench 为评估知识图谱集成流水线提供了一个标准化的框架，能够有效地量化不同流水线设计对最终知识图谱质量的影响，对于提升数据集成任务的自动化和决策水平具有重要意义。

Abstract: Integrating new data into knowledge graphs (KG) typically involves different tasks that are executed within workflows or pipelines There are many possible pipelines for a specific integration problem but there is not yet a general approach to evaluate the overall quality and performance of such pipelines to be able to determine the best choices. We therefore propose a new benchmark KGI-Bench to evaluate integration pipelines that ingest different kinds of input data into an existing KG. We evaluate pipelines by analyzing their output, i.e., the updated KG, with the three complementary quality metrics coverage, correctness and consistency. We also provide benchmark datasets (seed KG, overlapping input data of three formats, reference KG as a ground truth) for the movie domain. To demonstrate the applicability and usefulness of the proposed benchmark, we comparatively evaluate 12 pipelines and analyze their behavior across different input data formats and design choices.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在不确定领域中，为智能体部署感知能力时，需要在任务达成率与硬件及计算成本之间取得平衡。现有的最优可观测性问题（OOP）求解方法在规模化方面存在瓶颈，亟需提升求解效率。

Method: 本文提出了两种改进方案：一是改进了基于参数合成（parameter synthesis）的原始方法；二是开发了一种基于POMDP分解（decomposition）的新型求解方法，旨在通过结构化拆解来识别合理的观测函数。

Result: 实验结果表明，新方法在实例规模处理能力上提升了3个数量级，在计算运行时效上提升了5个数量级，显著超越了传统方法。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用POMDP分解技术可以极大地提升解决传感器选择问题（SSP）和位置可观测性问题（POP）的效率，为在复杂和不确定环境下优化智能体的感知部署提供了更具扩展性的解决方案。

Abstract: Deciding which sensing capabilities to deploy on an agent in uncertain domains is a fundamental engineering challenge, in which one balances task achievability against the high costs of hardware and processing. This problem has previously been formalized as the Optimal Observability Problem (OOP), based on the well-known Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) model for decision-making. This work studies (sub-)symbolic techniques to scale solving of decidable fragments of the OOP, namely the Sensor Selection Problem (SSP) and the Positional Observability Problem (POP). Besides improving the original approach based on parameter synthesis, we develop a new solving method that identifies sensible observation functions via decomposition of POMDPs, improving performance by 3 and 5 orders of magnitude for instance size and runtime, respectively.

Conclusion: Epicure 提供了一套跨语言、多维度的成分嵌入模型，通过融合烹饪语境和化学性质，能够有效地捕捉成分间的深层关联。该研究证明了结合共现数据与化学知识图谱对于构建高质量食品科学表征的有效性，为后续的食品科学和营养学计算研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: We present Epicure, a family of three sibling skip-gram ingredient embeddings retrained from scratch on a multilingual recipe corpus. We aggregate 4.14M recipes from 11 sources spanning seven languages, English, Chinese, Russian, Vietnamese, Spanish, Turkish, Indonesian, German, and Indian-English, and normalise the raw ingredient strings to 1,790 canonical entries via an LLM-augmented pipeline. A 203,508-edge ingredient-ingredient NPMI graph and an 80,019-edge typed FlavorDB ingredient-compound graph, 2,247 typed compound nodes across 15 categories, seed three Metapath2Vec variants that share architecture and hyperparameters and differ only in the random-walk schema: Cooc walks the co-occurrence graph only, Chem walks the typed compound metapaths only, and Core blends both via injected ingredient-ingredient walks at controlled mixing, placing each model at a distinct point on the chemistry-vs-recipe-context spectrum.

### [214] [S2ED: From Story to Executable Descriptions for Consistency-Aware Story Illustration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22448)
*Sijing Yin,Jiamou Liu,Xiao Tang,Yaser Shakib,Qian Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: S2ED 是一种无需训练的提示工程框架，它通过将故事转化为结构化的可执行描述，有效解决了多帧图像生成中角色一致性、场景布局和叙事逻辑难以维持的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的文本到图像生成模型难以在多帧故事插图中保持长距离的连贯性，特别是在角色身份持久性、场景布局和情感表现的跨帧一致性方面表现不足。目前的解决方案往往依赖于昂贵的训练过程，缺乏灵活性和可解释性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 S2ED（Story-to-Executable Descriptions）的训练无关、模型不可知的提示层框架。该框架利用三个协同智能体对故事进行叙事分解、标准化字符属性映射，并增强空间与情感线索。通过这种方式，将全篇故事转化为一系列可编辑、可执行的描述，从而实现可解释的状态传播，并通过局部编辑修正生成漂移。

Result: 在 Flintstones 和 Shakoo Maku 数据集上的实验结果表明，与强提示基线、大模型规划方法及参考训练方法相比，S2ED 在序列一致性和角色忠实度方面均有显著提升。该框架已被成功应用于儿童绘本生成系统，验证了其实际应用价值。

Conclusion: S2ED 框架通过引入可执行的描述层，为解决多帧故事插图中的长序列一致性问题提供了一种有效且高效的训练无关方案，展示了在保持字符一致性和叙事逻辑方面的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Multi-frame story illustration requires long-horizon coherence beyond single-image text-to-image generation, including narrative decomposition and persistent character identity, layout, and affect across frames. We propose Story-to-Executable Descriptions (S2ED), a training-free, model-agnostic, prompt-layer framework that converts a full story into a sequence of explicit, editable executable descriptions for more consistent rendering. S2ED coordinates three agents to segment the narrative, ground canonical character attributes, and enrich spatial and affective cues, enabling interpretable prompt-carried state propagation and local edits to repair drift without retraining the generator. Experiments on Flintstones and Shakoo Maku show that S2ED improves sequence-level consistency and character fidelity over strong prompting, large-model planning, and a reference training-based method, under both automatic metrics and human judgments. We also deploy S2ED in an end-to-end story-to-storybook system for children's illustrated stories, with a supplementary video.

### [215] [KAPPS: A knowledge-based CPPS Architecture for the Circular Factory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22457)
*Etienne Hoffmann,Jan-Felix Klein,Sören Weindel,Max Goebels,Sebastian Behrendt,Daniel Hernández,Ratan Bahadur Thapa,Jürgen Fleischer,Kai Furmans,Steffen Staab*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 为了解决循环制造中产品状态高度不确定和异构性带来的挑战，本文提出了基于知识图谱的 KAPPS 制造架构，通过语义集成与动态规划实现制造流程的灵活适应与人机知识交互，克服了传统制造 IT 系统的刚性限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 循环制造要求系统能够处理回收产品的高度不确定性与异构性，而传统制造 IT 架构依赖于预定义的顺序与同质化材料，无法应对运行时个体组件的独特性及动态变化的加工需求。因此，需要一种能够整合人机知识、实现动态可重构的新型架构。

Method: 采用设计科学研究方法论，首先从五个维度推导并确立了 14 项关键需求；基于此，设计并实现了 KAPPS（知识驱动的控制架构），该架构利用本体驱动的知识图谱作为核心数据骨干，结合语义接口层、约束执行模块及事件驱动规划模块，支持异构系统间的数据集成、推理与动态任务调整。

Result: 提出了 KAPPS 架构，并在两个实际案例中进行了验证：一是通过知识图谱中介服务进行异常检测与学习；二是在模块化传送系统中进行运行时约束执行。评估表明，KAPPS 能够满足循环制造的 14 项特定需求。

Conclusion: KAPPS 架构通过基于本体的知识图谱实现了制造系统的高度灵活性与动态适应性，有效弥合了传统制造 IT 架构在处理循环制造不确定性时的鸿沟，证明了知识驱动架构在处理异构、复杂回收产品过程中的可行性与优越性。

Abstract: While linear manufacturing relies on homogeneous materials and predefined process sequences, circular manufacturing reintroduces used products with heterogeneous and uncertain conditions. This shift demands manufacturing systems capable of handling variable product states, dynamically reconfigurable processes, and the integration of human and machine knowledge. Conventional manufacturing IT architectures, designed for stable structures and deterministic execution, are unable to meet these requirements, as they cannot adequately represent and manage the uniqueness of individual components at runtime. Following a design science methodology for developing a Cyber Physical Production System for circular manufacturing, we derive 14 requirements from five complementary perspectives. Based on these requirements, we design KAPPS, a knowledge-based architecture that uses an ontology-grounded knowledge graph as a unifying data backbone, combined with a semantic interface layer to enable consistent data and information integration, reasoning, and communication across heterogeneous systems and services, turning the knowledge graph from an integration layer into the factories authoritative write-time state. KAPPS incorporates modules for constraint enforcement and event-driven planning, enabling incremental adaptation of execution plans under uncertainty and human-machine knowledge exchange. The applicability of KAPPS is demonstrated through two implemented use cases: (i) Anomaly detection and learning through knowledge graph mediated services and (ii) runtime constraint enforcement in a modular conveyor system. Subsequently, the architecture is evaluated against the 14 requirements (ed. abstract shortened)

</details>

Result: 实证结果表明，将复杂程序（多达55个节点）编译进小模型是可行的。相比传统的编排框架，“地下智能体”在执行复杂任务时不仅具备相当的可靠性，且无需调用昂贵的超大模型，同时保护了程序的知识产权。

Conclusion: 通过实证研究，本文证明了将程序逻辑编译入小模型的“地下智能体”（Subterranean Agents）方案在效率、成本和隐私方面均优于传统的编排框架。作者呼吁开发者改变范式，通过微调取代冗余的运行时编排。

Abstract: Agent orchestration frameworks have proliferated, collectively exceeding 290,000 GitHub stars across LangGraph, CrewAI, Google ADK, OpenAI Agents SDK, Semantic Kernel, Strands, and LlamaIndex. All follow the same pattern: an external orchestrator above the LLM, injecting instructions and routing decisions every turn. Recent work has shown this architecture is dominated for procedural tasks by simply providing the procedure in a frontier model's system prompt [Dennis et al., 2026a], at the cost of consuming the context window, requiring a frontier model for every conversation, and exposing proprietary procedures to third-party providers. Compiling the procedure into the weights of a small fine-tuned model -- creating a subterranean agent -- should resolve all of these concerns, and prior work (SimpleTOD, FireAct, SynTOD, WorkflowLLM, Agent Lumos) has shown the technique works. Yet developer adoption has overwhelmingly favored orchestration. ### [217] [LACO: Adaptive Latent Communication for Collaborative Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22504)

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于语言的协作驾驶方法存在两个主要瓶颈：自回归解码带来的高延迟，以及将复杂表征压缩为离散词元导致的严重信息损失；此外，直接融合潜在状态会导致多智能体间的“智能体身份混淆”。

Method: 提出名为 LACO 的潜在通信范式，包含三个核心组件：1. 迭代潜在深思（ILD）：实现基于潜在空间的协同推理；2. 跨视界显著性归因（CHSA）：选择关键信息以提升通信效率；3. 结构化语义知识蒸馏（SSKD）：确保自我中心决策的稳定性。

Result: 在 CARLA 闭环模拟实验中，LACO 显著降低了通信与推理延迟，并在保持强劲协作驾驶性能的同时，克服了直接特征融合带来的决策纠缠问题。

Conclusion: LACO 证明了在协作驾驶中，通过无需训练的潜在空间通信范式（LACO），可以在无需昂贵的语言模型推理的情况下，解决多智能体通信中的身份混淆问题，并显著降低通信延迟，同时保持高性能的协作驾驶能力。

Abstract: Collaborative driving aims to improve safety and efficiency by enabling connected vehicles to coordinate under partial observability. Recent approaches have evolved from sharing visual features for perception to exchanging language-based reasoning through foundation models for behavioral coordination. Though communicating in language provides intuitive information, it introduces two challenges: high latency caused by autoregressive decoding and information loss caused by compressing rich internal representations into discrete tokens. To address these challenges, we analyze latent communication in collaborative driving under inherent limitations of multi-agent settings. Our analysis reveals agent identity confusion, where direct fusion of latent states entangles decision representations across vehicles. Motivated by this, we propose LACO, a training-free \textbf{LA}tent \textbf{CO}mmunication paradigm that seamlessly adapts pretrained driving models to collaborative settings. LACO introduces Iterative Latent Deliberation (ILD) for latent reasoning, Cross-Horizon Saliency Attribution (CHSA) for communication-efficient information selection, and Structured Semantic Knowledge Distillation (SSKD) to stabilize ego-centric decision making. Closed-loop experiments in CARLA show that LACO notably reduces communication and inference latency while maintaining strong collaborative driving performance.

### [218] [A Subjective Logic-based method for runtime confidence updates in safety arguments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22530)
*Benjamin Herd,Jessica Kelly,Clarissa Heinemann,João-Vitor Zacchi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于主观逻辑的动态安全保障方法，通过将实时运行指标集成到静态安全论证中，实现对系统置信度的连续更新，从而更有效地评估机器学习等组件在实际运行中的安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的静态安全论证无法适应系统运行环境的动态变化，且难以将机器学习组件的运行表现实时纳入安全评估中。研究旨在通过结合运行阶段的证据，建立一种能动态更新置信度的定量保障框架，以提升对复杂动态系统的安全评估能力。

Method: 提出了一种基于主观逻辑（Subjective Logic, SL）的动态定量保障方法：1. 将设计阶段的证据与运行阶段的窗口化安全性能指标（SPI）集成；2. 建立一种置信度传播规则，在无违规时增加置信度，在出现违规时迅速降低置信度；3. 优先考虑安全响应的实时性，而非追求传统贝叶斯后验更新的精确性。

Result: 通过施工区域辅助功能的仿真实验验证了该方法，结果表明，该框架能够根据施工锥检测组件的运行表现（SPI证据）实时更新置信度，在面对实际操作中的系统行为时，置信度的演变能够快速反映系统的安全状态。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入主观逻辑（SL），成功将静态安全论证扩展为能够根据实时证据动态调整置信度的评估框架。该方法有效地填补了开发阶段的安全论证与运行阶段实际表现之间的鸿沟，为机器学习等复杂系统的安全保障提供了一种兼顾响应速度与置信度更新的实用机制。

Abstract: We present a method for dynamic quantitative assurance that enhances static safety cases with continuous, runtime-driven confidence updates. The method quantifies and propagates confidence across the development lifecycle by integrating design-time evidence and windowed runtime Safety Performance Indicators (SPIs) within a single Subjective Logic (SL)-based assurance case. At runtime, SPI evidence is continuously evaluated, and targeted claims are updated using a rule that increases confidence in the absence of violations and imposes prompt penalties when violations occur. This design prioritizes safety-relevant responsiveness over exact classical Bayesian posterior updates. We demonstrate the method using a simulation-based construction zone assist function, focusing on an ML-based construction cone detection component, and show how confidence evolves as SPI evidence is observed in operation.

*Zhaoyang Chu,Jiarui Hu,Xingyu Jiang,Pengyu Zou,Han Li,Chao Peng,Peter O'Hearn,Earl T. Barr,Mark Harman,Federica Sarro,He Ye*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: TerminalWorld 是一个自动化数据引擎，通过挖掘真实的终端操作记录，创建了一个大规模、高保真的智能体评估基准。研究发现，即使是顶尖的智能体在处理复杂的现实终端工作流时表现仍然受限，且该基准与现有测试集存在显著差异，体现了其在评估真实世界能力方面的不可替代性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的专家策划类终端基准测试往往无法覆盖真实世界的复杂场景，且难以跟上开发者实践的快速迭代。为了弥补这一鸿沟，作者旨在开发一种可扩展的、自动化的方法，从真实的终端操作记录中提取真实的任务，从而实现对智能体在真实终端环境下的准确评估。

Method: 提出了一种名为 TerminalWorld 的自动化数据引擎，通过对 80,870 条“野外（in-the-wild）”终端录制数据进行逆向工程，自动提取并验证高保真的评估任务。该方法通过自动化流程处理复杂的工作流，并从中筛选出 200 个高质量的“Verified”人工审核任务集。

Result: 构建了包含 1,530 个验证任务的完整基准，并从中提取了 200 个经人工审核的 Verified 子集。对八个前沿模型和六个智能体的评测显示，最高通过率仅为 62.5%。此外，该基准与现有专家策划的基准（如 Terminal-Bench）的相关性极弱（Pearson r=0.20），证明了其独特且真实的评估价值。

Conclusion: TerminalWorld 揭示了现有大模型和智能体在处理真实终端工作流时存在显著瓶颈，强调了基于真实场景数据构建评估基准的必要性，并提供了一个可持续扩展的评估框架以应对开发者实践的不断演变。

Abstract: We introduce TerminalWorld, a scalable data engine that automatically reverse-engineers high-fidelity evaluation tasks from "in-the-wild" terminal recordings. Processing 80,870 terminal recordings, the engine yields a full benchmark of 1,530 validated tasks, spanning 18 real-world categories, ranging from short everyday operations to workflows exceeding 50 steps, and covering 1,280 unique commands. From these, we curate a Verified subset of 200 representative, manually reviewed tasks. Comprehensive benchmarking on TerminalWorld-Verified across eight frontier models and six agents reveals that current systems still struggle with authentic terminal workflows, achieving a maximum pass rate of only 62.5%. Moreover, TerminalWorld captures real-world terminal capabilities distinct from existing expert-curated benchmarks (e.g., Terminal-Bench), with only a weak correlation to their scores (Pearson r=0.20). The automated engine makes TerminalWorld authentic and scalable by construction, enabling it to evaluate agents in real-world terminal environments as developer practices evolve. Data and code are available at https://github.com/EuniAI/TerminalWorld.

*Minghui Ma,Bin Guo,Runze Yang,Mengqi Chen,Yan Liu,Jingqi Liu,Yahan Pei,Xuehao Ma,Qiuyun Zhang,Zhiwen Yu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Persuasive dialogue requires reasoning about others' latent mental states, a capability known as Theory of Mind (ToM). However, due to reliance on simple prompting strategies and insufficient ToM knowledge, existing LLMs often fail to capture the intrinsic dependencies among mental states, leading to fragmented representations and unstable reasoning. To address these challenges, we introduce the ToM-based Persuasive Dialogue (ToM-PD) task, grounded in the Belief-Desire-Intention (BDI) framework, which explicitly models the sequential dependencies among mental states in multi-turn dialogues. To facilitate research on this task, we construct a large-scale annotated dataset, ToM-based Broad Persuasive Dialogues (ToM-BPD), capturing fine-grained mental states and corresponding persuasive strategies. We further propose Think Thrice Before You Speak (TTBYS), a knowledge-enhanced stepwise reasoning framework that leverages both explicit and implicit prior experiences to improve LLMs' inference of desires, beliefs, and persuasive strategies. Experimental results demonstrate that Qwen3-8B equipped with TTBYS outperforms GPT-5 by 1.20%, 22.80%, and 16.97% in predicting desires, beliefs, and persuasive strategies, respectively. Case studies further show that our approach enhances interpretability and consistency in reasoning.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: Claude系列模型在基准测试中表现最佳，且输出结果最符合专业水准；然而，即使是性能最强的智能体，在面对超过少数简单链式计算的复杂任务时，表现也会显著下降，难以达到专业的金融标准。

Abstract: LLM agents are increasingly expected to carry out end-to-end workflows, producing complete artifacts from high-level user instructions. To meet enterprise needs, frontier AI labs have developed agents that can construct entire spreadsheets from scratch. This is especially relevant in finance, where core workflows such as financial modeling, forecasting, and scenario analysis are commonly conducted through spreadsheets. Yet, existing spreadsheet benchmarks do not measure this advanced capability, focusing instead on question-answering or single-formula edits. To address this gap, we provide one of the first evaluations of agents on end-to-end spreadsheet tasks, focusing on economically critical financial workflows such as modeling and scenario analysis. Since deliverables therein are routinely reviewed and revised by multiple stakeholders, judging their quality necessarily involves high-level criteria such as readability or ease of modification. This suggests that current agents are not yet able to reliably produce professional-quality spreadsheets at the level of complexity real-world workflows demand.

### [222] [Is Capability a Liability? More Capable Language Models Make Worse Forecasts When It Matters Most](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22672)
*Nick Merrill,Jaeho Lee,Ezra Karger*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了大型语言模型在处理具有超线性增长和高尾部风险的预测任务时，存在能力越强、预测表现越差的“反向扩展”现象，指出传统评估指标会掩盖该问题，并建议采用更全面的连续准确性评估方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究人员观察到大模型在特定预测任务（如金融或流行病学中具有超线性增长和制度突变风险的序列）中表现出异常的行为。现有的评估方法通常基于单阈值指标，可能无法捕捉到模型在高风险尾部预测上的错误，因此旨在揭示并量化这种“反向扩展”现象。

Method: 1. 构建了无污染的模拟世界基准测试集（ForecastBench-Sim, FBSim）；2. 对比了合成SIR流行病数据与线性对照组的表现；3. 在COVID-19、麻疹、房地产市场和恶性通胀等真实数据集上进行验证；4. 采用分位数分解法（per-quantile decomposition）分析预测偏差；5. 使用Llama-3.1模型家族进行模型规模与后训练对性能影响的对照研究；6. 对比了单阈值指标与尾部包含指标对模型评估的影响。

Result: 研究发现，随着模型能力的提升，其在预测分布的高尾部表现出向上的过度偏移，导致预测准确性下降；即使使用领域知识也无法可靠地解决校准偏差问题；该现象在单阈值指标下被隐藏，但在尾部包含（tail-inclusive）的评估指标下表现显著。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型（LLM）在处理具有超线性增长和尾部风险的预测任务时存在“反向扩展”现象，即模型能力越强，分布预测效果反而越差。研究强调，现有的单阈值评估指标会掩盖这一问题，因此必须引入连续且无界的准确性评估指标，才能准确反映模型在复杂预测任务中的真实性能。

Abstract: We document inverse scaling in LLMs on forecasting problems whose underlying time series exhibit superlinear growth and tail risk of regime change, a structure common in finance and epidemiology. On these tasks, more capable models produce worse distributional forecasts. The pattern appears on ForecastBench-Sim (FBSim), a contamination-free, simulated-world benchmark we release, in forecasting synthetic SIR epidemics with a matched linear control, and replicates in real-world datasets on COVID-19, measles, housing markets, and hyperinflation. A per-quantile decomposition shows the failure concentrates at the upper tail, which more capable models shift upward to track aggressive extrapolations of growth, while the lower tail stays put. A within-family study of Llama-3.1 shows that both model scale and post-training independently contribute to this effect. Domain knowledge does not reliably rescue calibration. This inverse scaling does not appear on single-threshold metrics common in LLM forecasting benchmarks, reversing the sign of the capability--accuracy relationship on identical outputs. Single-threshold scoring at conventional cutoffs misses the upper-tail cost; tail-inclusive scoring reverses the sign of the capability--accuracy relationship on the same outputs. We recommend that LLM forecasting evaluations use continuous (and unbounded) measures of accuracy alongside bounded binary threshold metrics.

</details>


### [223] [Forecasting Scientific Progress with Artificial Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22681)
*Sean Wu,Pan Lu,Yupeng Chen,Jonathan Bragg,Yutaro Yamada,Peter Clark,David Clifton,Philip Torr,James Zou,Junchi Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究引入了CUSP基准框架，系统评估了AI在预测科学进步方面的能力，发现当前AI模型难以可靠地预测科学发现的可行性与时间，且存在显著的过信和推理偏差，难以作为科学预测工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管AI在科学发现中应用日益广泛，但AI系统是否具备“预测科学进步”的能力尚不明确。因此，研究旨在量化AI预测科学发现的可行性、时间和机理的能力，以探究AI在科学前瞻性研究中的实际效用。

Method: 构建了一个名为CUSP（Cutoff-conditioned Unseen Scientific Progress）的评估框架，该框架是一个多学科、事件级的基准测试，涵盖可行性评估、机理推理、生成式解决方案设计及时间预测四个维度。研究团队通过该框架在4760个科学事件上对前沿模型进行了受控知识约束的对比测试。

Result: 测试结果显示：1. 模型在识别潜在研究方向上表现尚可，但在判断科学进展是否会实现以及何时实现方面表现较差；2. 预测性能在不同学科间存在显著差异（AI领域预测较准，生物、化学和物理领域较难）；3. 模型的预测能力受训练数据截断点的影响较小，表明其局限性并非仅由知识缺失导致；4. 模型存在严重的过信倾向，缺乏有效的不确定性评估能力。

Conclusion: 现有的前沿AI系统尚不足以成为预测科学进步的可靠工具。研究表明，AI模型在科学预测方面的表现不仅受限于训练数据的知识覆盖，还存在严重的过信偏见和推理能力缺失，无法有效判断科学发现的可行性及其实际发生的时间点。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) is increasingly embedded in scientific discovery, yet whether it can anticipate scientific progress remains unclear. To study this question, we introduce a temporally grounded evaluation framework for forecasting scientific progress under controlled knowledge constraints. We present CUSP (Cutoff-conditioned Unseen Scientific Progress), a multi-disciplinary and event-level benchmark that evaluates scientific forecasting in AI systems through feasibility assessment, mechanistic reasoning, generative solution design, and temporal prediction. Across 4,760 scientific events, we observe systematic and domain-dependent limitations in current frontier models. While models can identify plausible research directions from competing candidates, they fail to reliably predict whether scientific advances will be realized and systematically misestimate when they will occur. Performance is highly heterogeneous across domains, with the timing of AI progress more predictable than advances in biology, chemistry, and physics. Performance is largely insensitive to whether events occur before or after the training cutoff, suggesting these limitations cannot be explained solely by knowledge exposure in training data. Under controlled information access, additional pre-cutoff knowledge improves performance but does not close the gap to full-information settings, which becomes more pronounced for high-citation advances. Models also exhibit systematic overconfidence and strong response biases, indicating unreliable uncertainty estimation. Taken together, current AI systems fall short as predictive tools for scientific progress. Access to prior knowledge does not translate into reliable forecasting, and performance benefits more from post-event information than from forward-looking prediction.

</details>


### [224] [Beyond the Org Chart: AI and the Transformation of Invisible Work](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22707)
*Stephanie Rosenthal,Shamsi Iqbal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了AI如何重塑企业职场，指出尽管AI提升了协作效率，但却削弱了职场导师制、知识传承和职业成长等关键文化实践，研究呼吁企业应采取措施使这些“隐性工作”重获重视。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI在企业中的广泛应用不仅改变了正式的岗位职责，也潜移默化地影响了职业发展所需的隐性文化实践（如导师制）。研究旨在揭示这种变化对员工职业成长、团队协作及公司文化的潜在影响。

Method: 研究团队对一家大型科技公司的24名产品相关人员进行了深入访谈，通过质性研究方法探讨AI应用如何重塑了个体工作内容、团队协作流程以及职场人际互动方式。

Result: 研究发现，AI虽然提升了部分协作效率，但也弱化了职场中的隐性社会资本积累，导致反馈机制受损，导师制和领导力培养面临挑战。这些关键的职业成长路径正在因为AI的过度介入而变得边缘化。

Conclusion: AI技术对企业职场文化和职业发展构成了深远挑战。企业若要保持健康的协作文化和多样性思维，必须主动干预，通过提高“隐性工作”的可见度，并建立新的机制来支持导师制与领导力培养，以应对技术变革带来的负面影响。

Abstract: An increasing number of news and research articles report that AI adoption is allowing professionals to blur and extend the boundaries of their corporate roles. With the goal of understanding how work processes might be changing in an AI-forward company, we interviewed 24 product-focused individuals at a large technology firm about how AI has impacted their own work, their work within their product team, and their professional interactions. Our conversations suggest that AI is not only changing formal role responsibilities and collaborations between those roles, but also changing informal cultural practices like professional mentoring that are key to helping professionals settle in their positions, stay engaged with their work, and grow their careers. Some of these changes are positive, such as smoother collaboration between peers, but other changes are more nuanced and put the typical career growth opportunities, like receiving feedback from professional networks and promoting leadership and mentorship, at risk. We propose steps that AI companies can take to make the invisible work more visible. Additionally, we propose efforts that individuals and leaders can take to support their colleagues through AI transformation while preserving healthy company cultures that support diverse thinking, collaboration, and informal interactions.

### [225] [AMEL: Accumulated Message Effects on LLM Judgments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22714)
*Sid-ali Temkit*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究发现大语言模型在连续评估任务中存在“累积消息效应”（AMEL），即先前的对话历史会严重干扰模型的后续判断，尤其是当模型本身不确定时，且模型对负面历史更敏感。该偏见无法通过单纯增大模型规模解决，建议在实际应用中采用“单项独立上下文”的策略进行优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）常被用于自动化评估任务（如代码审查、内容审核等），通常涉及在单次会话中处理大量任务。研究者旨在探究模型在处理这类长对话序列时，先前的对话历史是否会对后续的判断产生偏见，即所谓的“累积消息效应”（AMEL）。

Method: 研究人员通过调用4个供应商（OpenAI, Anthropic, Google及开源模型）的11种模型，共计进行了75,898次API调用。实验设计将相同的测试项分别置于“中立环境（孤立测试）”以及“充满正向或负向评估的历史上下文”中进行对比，分析不同历史环境对模型后续判断的影响，并探究了上下文长度、模型规模及位置对该偏见的影响机制。

Result: 1. 普遍存在偏见：模型判断显著向历史极性偏移（d = -0.17）。
2. 不确定性依赖：该效应在模型基准不确定性高（高熵）的任务中更为严重。
3. 对称性缺失：负面历史引发的偏见是正面的1.62倍。
4. 长度与位置无关：偏见程度不随历史长度增加，且5轮历史在长序列中的任何位置产生的影响一致。
5. 模型规模：Scaling（模型扩展）能轻微缓解但无法解决此问题。

Conclusion: LLM在执行评估任务时存在显著的“累积消息效应”（AMEL），即先前的对话历史会偏向性地影响模型对后续内容的判断。该效应在模型本身不确定性较高时更为明显，且存在显著的负面偏见不对称性。通过为每个任务项提供独立的上下文环境或平衡对话历史，可以有效缓解此偏见，仅靠增加模型参数规模无法完全消除该问题。

Abstract: Large language models are routinely used as automated evaluators: to review code, moderate content, or score outputs, often with many items passing through one conversation. We ask whether the polarity of prior conversation history biases subsequent judgments, an effect we call the accumulated message effect on LLM judgments (AMEL). Across 75,898 API calls to 11 models from 4 providers (OpenAI, Anthropic, Google, and four open-source models), we present identical test items in isolation or following histories saturated with predominantly positive or negative evaluations.
  Models shift toward the conversation's prevailing polarity (d = -0.17, p < 10^-46). The effect concentrates on items where the model is genuinely uncertain at baseline (d = -0.34 for high-entropy items, vs d = -0.15 when the baseline is deterministic). Bias does not grow with context length: 5 prior turns and 50 produce the same shift (Spearman |r| < 0.01; OLS slope p = 0.80). And there is a negativity asymmetry: paired per item, negative histories induce 1.62x more bias than positive (t = 13.46, p < 10^-39, n = 2,481). Scaling helps but does not solve it (Anthropic: Haiku -0.22 to Opus -0.17; OpenAI: Nano -0.34 to GPT-5.2 -0.17).
  Three follow-ups narrow the mechanism. The token probability distribution shifts continuously, not at a threshold. The negativity asymmetry has both token-level and semantic components, though attributing the balance is exploratory at our sample sizes. Position does not matter: five biased turns anywhere in a 50-turn history produce the same shift. The simplest fix for evaluation pipelines is a fresh context per item; when batching is unavoidable, balancing the history helps.

</details>


### [226] [Parametric Modular Answer Set Programs Made Declarative](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22716)
*Jorge Fandinno,Yuliya Lierler,Torsten Schaub*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种模块化一阶回答集程序（ASP）的新形式——参数化模块逻辑程序，通过引入参数与内涵声明，实现了更高级的子程序结构化管理与实例化控制，提升了复杂逻辑程序的建模能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解决当前一阶回答集程序（ASP）在复杂系统建模中缺乏模块化机制的问题，提高程序的结构化程度、复用性及子程序的实例化控制能力。

Method: 提出了一种名为“参数化模块逻辑程序”（parametric modular logic programs）的新形式化方法，通过引入参数和内涵性声明来定义子程序，并展示了其如何捕捉clingo程序中集体控制的语义。

Result: 建立了模块化ASP的理论基础，证明了该形式化方法能够有效表示具有集体控制功能的clingo程序，并明确了其与传统非模块化ASP之间的逻辑关联。

Conclusion: 该论文为一阶回答集程序（ASP）奠定了模块化理论基础，提出的参数化模块逻辑程序提供了一种结构化、可复用且具有可控性的建模方式，有效填补了模块化理论与实际ASP应用之间的差距。

Abstract: In this paper, we explore the concept of modularity in first-order answer set programming (ASP). We introduce a new formalism called parametric modular logic programs, which allows defining subprograms with parameters and intensionality statements. We demonstrate how this formalism can capture the semantics of clingo-programs with collective control, a feature that enables structuring and instantiating subprograms. We provide theoretical foundations for modular ASP, illustrate its usefulness, and connect to traditional non-modular ASP.

### [227] [Can AI Make Conflicts Worse? An Alignment Failure in LLM Deployment Across Conflict Contexts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22720)
*Andrii Kryshtal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文研究了AI模型在武装冲突语境下的安全性，通过评估九种主流模型发现其在应对暴行 denial、种族偏见及“虚假平衡”压力时表现不佳，并首次提出了一套专门用于评估冲突敏感性的对齐评估框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着人工智能被广泛应用于受武装冲突影响的社会，其潜在输出可能加剧冲突、破坏脆弱社会的稳定。目前尚无针对AI模型在冲突语境下安全性的成熟评估标准。

Method: 研究人员针对四个主流模型供应商（OpenAI, Anthropic, DeepSeek, xAI）的九种模型配置进行了测试。设计了90个多轮对话场景，重点测试模型在处理种族灭绝否认、暴行虚假对等、种族歧视用语等冲突敏感问题时的表现，并评估了用户施加“平衡”压力下的模型合规性。

Result: 研究发现模型表现参差不齐，失败率在6%到47%之间；在国际法院已定性的暴行场景中，当被要求“保持平衡”时，九种模型配置中有五种的失败率高达80%至100%。

Conclusion: 在冲突地区应用人工智能模型具有显著风险，若缺乏专门的对齐评估，模型输出可能加剧社会分裂。该研究强调将冲突敏感性评估纳入模型对齐体系的必要性。

Abstract: AI models are already deployed in societies affected by armed conflict, and journalists, humanitarian workers, governments and ordinary citizens rely on them for information or for their work processes. No established practice exists for checking whether their outputs can make those conflicts worse. We tested nine model configurations from four providers (OpenAI, Anthropic, DeepSeek, xAI) on 90 multi-turn scenarios designed to surface misaligned behaviour in conflict contexts: false equivalence between documented atrocities, denial of genocide, and failure to recognise ethnic slurs, among others. When such outputs feed into journalism, humanitarian reporting, or public debate, they can deepen divisions in fragile societies. Failure rates span 6\% to 47\% between the best and worst performing models, which makes model choice a safety question in its own right and when users pushed for ``balance'' in cases where international courts have already assigned responsibility, five of nine configurations failed 80 to 100 percent of the time. We release the first evaluation framework for this domain and propose adding it to alignment evaluation portfolios.

### [228] [LCGuard: Latent Communication Guard for Safe KV Sharing in Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22786)
*Sadia Asif,Mohammad Mohammadi Amiri,Momin Abbas,Prasanna Sattigeri,Karthikeyan Natesan Ramamurthy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对多智能体系统利用 KV 缓存进行隐式通信带来的隐私泄露风险，本文提出了 LCGuard 框架，通过对抗性训练对缓存数据进行表征转换，在确保任务效率的同时有效阻断了敏感信息的重构与传播。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）的多智能体系统逐渐采用 KV 缓存进行隐式通信以提高效率，但这会引发隐私安全问题——KV 缓存可能包含敏感的上下文输入和推理状态，且缺乏显式的安全控制，导致敏感信息在智能体间无意泄露。

Method: LCGuard 框架将共享 KV 缓存视为潜在工作记忆，并引入表征级转换机制。其核心方法是建立对抗性学习范式：通过模拟攻击者尝试从缓存中重构敏感输入，训练 LCGuard 执行信息转换，在保留任务相关语义信息的同时，最大限度地减少可重构的敏感信息。

Result: 实验表明，LCGuard 在多个模型系列和基准测试中，显著降低了基于重构的隐私泄露风险和攻击成功率，同时在任务性能上表现出与标准 KV 共享机制相当的竞争力。

Conclusion: LCGuard 证明了在多智能体系统中，通过对抗性训练对共享 KV 缓存进行表征级转换，可以在有效防御敏感信息泄露的同时，保持任务执行的性能，为构建安全、高效的隐式通信机制提供了可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based multi-agent systems increasingly rely on intermediate communication to coordinate complex tasks. While most existing systems communicate through natural language, recent work shows that latent communication, particularly through transformer key-value (KV) caches, can improve efficiency and preserve richer task-relevant information. However, KV caches also encode contextual inputs, intermediate reasoning states, and agent-specific information, creating an opaque channel through which sensitive content may propagate across agents without explicit textual disclosure. To address this, we introduce \textbf{LCGuard} (Latent Communication Guard), a framework for safe KV-based latent communication in multi-agent LLM systems. LCGuard treats shared KV caches as latent working memory and learns representation-level transformations before cache artifacts are transmitted across agents. We formalize representation-level sensitive information leakage operationally through reconstruction: a shared cache artifact is unsafe if an adversarial decoder can recover agent-specific sensitive inputs from it. This leads to an adversarial training formulation in which the adversary learns to reconstruct sensitive inputs, while LCGuard learns transformations that preserve task-relevant semantics and reduce reconstructable information. Empirical evaluations across multiple model families and multi-agent benchmarks show that LCGuard consistently reduces reconstruction-based leakage and attack success rates while maintaining competitive task performance compared to standard KV-sharing baselines.

</details>


### [229] [Gated DeltaNet-2: Decoupling Erase and Write in Linear Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22791)
*Ali Hatamizadeh,Yejin Choi,Jan Kautz*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Gated DeltaNet-2 改进了线性注意力机制，通过解耦“擦除”与“写入”操作，增强了模型的记忆编辑精度，从而在长上下文任务中实现了比 Mamba 系列更卓越的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的线性注意力模型（如 Gated DeltaNet 和 KDA）在通过 Delta 规则更新记忆时，通常使用单一标量门同时控制擦除和写入，限制了模型对复杂关联的记忆与遗忘能力，导致在处理长上下文时的检索表现受限。

Method: 提出 Gated DeltaNet-2，引入了通道维度的擦除门（erase gate）和写入门（write gate），将两者独立控制以解决 Gated DeltaNet 和 KDA 中标量耦合的局限性。同时，通过分块 WY 算法和门控感知的反向传播机制，实现了高效的并行训练和常数内存推理。

Result: 在 1.3B 参数量及 100B Token 的训练规模下，Gated DeltaNet-2 在语言建模、常识推理及 RULER 长上下文检索任务中均优于 Mamba-2、Gated DeltaNet 和 KDA 等基线模型。

Conclusion: Gated DeltaNet-2 通过将擦除和写入门的标量耦合解耦为通道维度的独立门控，成功优化了线性注意力机制的记忆更新能力。在多种规模和基准测试中，它展现了比 Mamba 和早期 Delta 规则模型更优的性能，证明了该架构在处理长上下文和复杂检索任务上的显著优势。

Abstract: Linear attention replaces the unbounded cache of softmax attention with a fixed-size recurrent state, reducing sequence mixing to linear time and decoding to constant memory. The hard part is not just what to forget, but how to edit this compressed memory without scrambling existing associations. Delta-rule models subtract the current read before writing a new value, and Kimi Delta Attention (KDA) sharpens forgetting with channel-wise decay. But the active edit still uses a single scalar gate to control two different things: how much old content to erase on the key side and how much new content to commit on the value side. We introduce Gated DeltaNet-2, which generalizes both Gated DeltaNet and KDA by inheriting adaptive forgetting and channel-wise decay while addressing their shared limitation, the scalar tie between erasing and writing. Gated Delta Rule-2 separates these roles with a channel-wise erase gate b_t and a channel-wise write gate w_t, reducing to KDA when both gates collapse to the same scalar and to Gated DeltaNet when the decay also collapses. We derive a fast-weight update view, a chunkwise WY algorithm with channel-wise decay absorbed into asymmetric erase factors, and a gate-aware backward pass that preserves efficient parallel training. At 1.3B parameters trained on 100B FineWeb-Edu tokens, Gated DeltaNet-2 achieves the strongest overall results among Mamba-2, Gated DeltaNet, KDA, and Mamba-3 variants across language modeling, commonsense reasoning, and retrieval. Its advantage is most pronounced on long-context RULER needle-in-a-haystack benchmarks, where it improves the evaluated multi-key retrieval setting and remains strong in both recurrent and hybrid settings. Code is available at https://github.com/NVlabs/GatedDeltaNet-2.

</details>


### [230] [MOSS: Self-Evolution through Source-Level Rewriting in Autonomous Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22794)
*Qianshu Cai,Yonggang Zhang,Xianzhang Jia,Wei Xue,Jun Song,Xinmei Tian,Yike Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对现有智能体无法自我修复代码级结构缺陷的问题，本文提出了 MOSS 系统，通过自动化、确定性的源代码重写与部署流程，使智能体能够直接在生产环境中进行深度进化，显著提高了系统的自我修复能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的智能体自我进化机制多局限于提示词、配置文件或记忆模式等文本层面的修改，无法解决代码结构层面（如路由、状态不变性、调度逻辑）导致的深层故障，且存在受基础模型依从性限制及长上下文漂移等问题。

Method: 提出了 MOSS 系统，该系统采用多阶段确定性流水线进行源代码级重写：首先自动归纳生产环境的失败证据，利用外部编程智能体（Coding-agent）进行代码修改，随后在临时环境回放验证候选版本，最后通过用户确认及健康检查机制实现无缝容器替换与回滚。

Result: MOSS 系统在 OpenClaw 测试集上实现了显著的性能提升，在无需人工干预的情况下，单次演化周期内将四个任务的平均评分从 0.25 提升至 0.61。

Conclusion: 本文证明了源代码级别的自我进化是提升智能体鲁棒性的有效且通用方案，通过将智能体演化从文本配置提升到代码逻辑层面，能够从根本上解决传统智能体在处理结构性故障时的局限性。

Abstract: Autonomous agentic systems are largely static after deployment: they do not learn from user interactions, and recurring failures persist until the next human-driven update ships a fix. Self-evolving agents have emerged in response, but all confine evolution to text-mutable artifacts -- skill files, prompt configurations, memory schemas, workflow graphs -- and leave the agent harness untouched. Since routing, hook ordering, state invariants, and dispatch live in code rather than in any text artifact, an entire class of structural failure is physically unreachable from the text layer. We argue that source-level adaptation is a fundamentally more general medium: it is Turing-complete, a strict superset of every text-mutable scope, takes effect deterministically rather than through base-model compliance, and does not erode under long-context drift. We present MOSS, a system that performs self-rewriting at the source level on production agentic substrates. Each evolution is anchored to an automatically curated batch of production-failure evidence and proceeds through a deterministic multi-stage pipeline; code modification is delegated to a pluggable external coding-agent CLI while MOSS retains stage ordering and verdicts. Candidates are verified by replaying the batch against the candidate image in ephemeral trial workers, then promoted via user-consent-gated, in-place container swap with health-probe-gated rollback. On OpenClaw, MOSS lifts a four-task mean grader score from 0.25 to 0.61 in a single cycle without human intervention.

</details>
